# I-arch-001f diff iter 1 — e2e test pinning POST → stream → resume → bundle

Brief APPROVE iter 3 of 5. This is the diff implementation.

## Diff: `.codex/I-arch-001f/codex_diff.patch` (~280 LOC, 1 NEW test file)

## File added (1)

**NEW `tests/v6/test_end_to_end_arch_001f.py`** (~280 LOC, 1 test):

`test_e2e_post_run_through_stream_resume_and_bundle` exercises the full I-arch-001a..001e chain:

1. POST `/runs` → 202 + uuid + `lifecycle_status="queued"`
2. Simulate pipeline-A side-effects: `_write_synthetic_artifact_dir(tmp_path)` (reused from I-arch-001d), patch manifest.json to thread `external_run_id`/`scope.decision_id`, then `run_store.mark_in_progress` + `run_store.set_pipeline_meta(**kwargs)` + `emit_event("scope_gate.completed")` + `emit_terminal_event("success")` + `run_store.mark_completed`
3. GET `/runs/{uuid}` → 200 + `lifecycle_status="completed"` + `pipeline_status="success"`
4. GET `/stream/{uuid}` (with monkeypatched `read_events` feeding fakeredis) → SSE: `scope_decision` + `run_complete` (translated from pipeline-A naming)
5. GET `/stream/{uuid}` with `Last-Event-ID: <first_event_id>` → only `run_complete` (resume semantics)
6. GET `/runs/{uuid}/bundle.tar.gz` with `dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn] = _stub_sign_fn` → not-503 (P1-001 regression check from I-arch-001d)
7. Open tar via `tarfile` + `BytesIO`; parse `audit_<id>/manifest.yaml` (yaml.safe_load) + `audit_<id>/verified_report.json`. Assert:
   - `bundle_manifest.report_id == bundle_report.report_id`
   - `bundle_manifest.decision_id == bundle_report.decision_id == f"dec-{posted_run_id}"`
   - `bundle_manifest.pool_id == bundle_report.pool_id` (if present)
   - Source `artifact_dir/manifest.json.external_run_id == posted_run_id`
   - `run_store.get_run(uuid).run_id == posted_run_id`

## P1 resolutions verified in code

- **P1-001 fixture run_id consistency:** lines 154-162 patch source manifest.json with posted UUID + decision_id + slug; `build_slice_chain` reads these into the slice chain.
- **P1-002 POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB isolation + StubBroker flush:** `isolated_runs_db` fixture (lines 47-53) uses `monkeypatch.setenv` + `run_store.init_db(tmp_path/...)`. `flush_stub_broker` autouse fixture (lines 57-68) calls `broker.flush_all()` before + after yield with `hasattr` guard.
- **P1-003 Last-Event-ID resume assertion:** lines 207-213 issue a SECOND GET with `Last-Event-ID: <first_event_id>` header, assert only `run_complete` returned.
- **P1-004 keyword-only set_pipeline_meta:** lines 168-175 call with all kwargs (query_slug, artifact_dir, manifest_run_id, decision_id, path).
- **P1-005 broker.flush_all (not flush_queue):** line 60-61 + 65-66 use `hasattr(broker, "flush_all")` guard then `broker.flush_all()`.
- **P1-006 manifest.yaml + verified_report.json:** lines 230-242 open tar, extract those two members, `yaml.safe_load` the manifest, assert FK chain. External_run_id asserted ONLY against source manifest.json + run_store record (lines 257-260), NOT against bundle manifest.

+"""I-arch-001f — end-to-end capstone test for the I-arch-001a..001e seam.
+
+POST /runs → simulate pipeline-A side-effects → GET /runs/{id} →
+GET /stream/{id} → GET /stream/{id} with Last-Event-ID resume →
+GET /runs/{id}/bundle.tar.gz → extract tar → cross-validate manifest.yaml
++ verified_report.json IDs.
+
+Hermetic via fakeredis + synthetic AuditIR fixture (no real Redis, no LLM,
+no network). Pins the I-arch-001a..001e architectural seam end-to-end so
+any future drift breaks one obvious assertion. Brief APPROVE iter 3 of 5
+at .codex/I-arch-001f/codex_brief_verdict_iter_3.txt.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import io
+import json
+import tarfile
+from pathlib import Path
+
+import pytest
+import yaml
+
+# Force StubBroker BEFORE importing actors / runs (tests/v6/conftest.py
+# already does this, but be defensive when this module is collected alone).
+pytest.importorskip("dramatiq")
+pytest.importorskip("fakeredis")

+pytest.importorskip("sse_starlette")

+# Reuse the synthetic AuditIR fixture builder from I-arch-001d tests.
+from tests.polaris_v6.api.test_artifact_to_slice_chain import (
+    _write_synthetic_artifact_dir,
+)

+@pytest.fixture
+def isolated_runs_db(tmp_path, monkeypatch):
+    """Per Codex iter-2 P1-002: isolate POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB so the test does NOT
+    write to state/v6_runs.sqlite or bleed into other tests."""
+    db_path = tmp_path / "e2e_v6_runs.sqlite"
+    monkeypatch.setenv("POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB", str(db_path))
+    run_store.init_db(str(db_path))
+    yield db_path
+

+@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
+def flush_stub_broker():
+    """Per Codex iter-3 P1-005: StubBroker uses flush_all(), not flush_queue().
+    Guarded by hasattr so a real-Redis broker (no flush_all) is a no-op."""
+    import dramatiq
+
+    broker = dramatiq.get_broker()
+    if hasattr(broker, "flush_all"):
+        broker.flush_all()
+    yield
+    if hasattr(broker, "flush_all"):
+        broker.flush_all()

+    import fakeredis
+

+    import fakeredis
+
+    return fakeredis.FakeStrictRedis(server=fake_server)

+@pytest.fixture
+def async_fake(fake_server):
+    import fakeredis
+
+    return fakeredis.aioredis.FakeRedis(server=fake_server)

+@pytest.fixture
+def app_with_v6_routers(isolated_runs_db):
+    """Mount the v6 routers needed for the e2e chain: runs, stream, bundle."""
+    from fastapi import FastAPI
+    from polaris_v6.api import bundle as bundle_module
+    from polaris_v6.api import runs as runs_module
+    from polaris_v6.api import stream as stream_module
+
+    app = FastAPI()
+    app.include_router(runs_module.router)
+    app.include_router(stream_module.router)
+    app.include_router(bundle_module.router)
+    return app

+def _stub_sign_fn():
+    """Per I-arch-001d test_get_bundle_targz_signer_override_fires."""
+    def _sign(_data: bytes) -> bytes:
+        return b"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\nstub\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n"
+
+    return _sign
+
+
+def _parse_sse_block(raw: str) -> list[dict]:
+    """Parse SSE wire format into list of dicts with optional id/event/data."""
+    normalized = raw.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")
+    events: list[dict] = []
+    for block in normalized.split("\n\n"):
+        block = block.strip()
+        if not block:
+            continue
+        evt: dict = {}
+        for line in block.splitlines():
+            line = line.strip()
+            if line.startswith(":"):
+                continue
+            if line.startswith("event:"):
+                evt["event"] = line[len("event:"):].strip()
+            elif line.startswith("data:"):
+                evt["data"] = json.loads(line[len("data:"):].strip())
+            elif line.startswith("id:"):
+                evt["id"] = line[len("id:"):].strip()
+        if evt.get("event"):
+            events.append(evt)
+    return events
+
+
+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+# E2E capstone test
+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

+def test_e2e_post_run_through_stream_resume_and_bundle(
+    app_with_v6_routers,
+    isolated_runs_db,
+    fake_server,
+    sync_fake,
+    async_fake,
+    tmp_path,
+    monkeypatch,
+):
+    """Capstone test pinning POST/runs → stream → resume → bundle chain."""
+    from fastapi.testclient import TestClient
+
+    client = TestClient(app_with_v6_routers)
+
+    # ----- Step 1: POST /runs ---------------------------------------------
+    create_resp = client.post(
+        "/runs", json={"template": "clinical", "question": "synthetic question"}
+    )
+    assert create_resp.status_code == 202, create_resp.text
+    create_body = create_resp.json()
+    posted_run_id = create_body["run_id"]
+    assert create_body["lifecycle_status"] == "queued"
+
+    # ----- Step 2: simulate pipeline-A side-effects -----------------------
+    # 2a. Build a synthetic AuditIR-shape artifact directory.
+    artifact_dir = _write_synthetic_artifact_dir(tmp_path)
+
+    # 2b. Patch the source manifest.json to thread the POST uuid + decision_id
+    #     consistently — per Codex iter-2 P1-001. The augment_v6_manifest helper
+    #     would normally do this inside pipeline-A; in the test we set the
+    #     final values directly so artifact_to_slice_chain produces a
+    #     ScopeDecision with our decision_id.
+    manifest_path = artifact_dir / "manifest.json"
+    src_manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+    src_manifest["external_run_id"] = posted_run_id
+    src_manifest["scope"]["decision_id"] = f"dec-{posted_run_id}"
+    src_manifest["slug"] = "synthetic_e2e"
+    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(src_manifest, sort_keys=True), encoding="utf-8")
+
+    # 2c. run_store transitions (the Phase-0 actor stub does NOT call these;
+    #     the real pipeline-A actor will).
+    run_store.mark_in_progress(posted_run_id, path=str(isolated_runs_db))
+    run_store.set_pipeline_meta(
+        posted_run_id,
+        query_slug="synthetic_e2e",
+        artifact_dir=str(artifact_dir),
+        manifest_run_id=src_manifest["run_id"],
+        decision_id=f"dec-{posted_run_id}",
+        path=str(isolated_runs_db),
+    )
+    # 2d. Emit pipeline-A events into fakeredis.
+    _run_events_module.emit_event(
+        posted_run_id,
+        "scope_gate.completed",
+        {"decision": "in_scope", "reason": "synthetic"},
+        redis_client=sync_fake,
+    )
+    _run_events_module.emit_terminal_event(
+        posted_run_id, "success", redis_client=sync_fake,
+    )
+    # 2e. Final run_store transition.
+    run_store.mark_completed(
+        posted_run_id,
+        {"manifest": {"status": "success"}, "status": "success"},
+        pipeline_status="success",
+        cost_usd=0.42,
+        path=str(isolated_runs_db),
+    )
+
+    # ----- Step 3: GET /runs/{id} -----------------------------------------
+    get_resp = client.get(f"/runs/{posted_run_id}")
+    assert get_resp.status_code == 200, get_resp.text
+    get_body = get_resp.json()
+    assert get_body["lifecycle_status"] == "completed"
+    assert get_body["pipeline_status"] == "success"
+
+    # ----- Step 4: GET /stream/{id} ---------------------------------------
+    # Monkeypatch stream module's read_events to feed pre-seeded fakeredis to
+    # the async reader (same pattern as I-arch-001e tests).
+    from polaris_v6.api import stream as stream_module
+    real_read = _run_events_module.read_events
+
+    async def _read_with_fake(run_id, last_event_id="0-0", *, block_ms=5000, redis_client_async=None):
+        async for sid, raw in real_read(
+            run_id, last_event_id=last_event_id, block_ms=50, redis_client_async=async_fake
+        ):
+            yield sid, raw
+
+    monkeypatch.setattr(stream_module, "read_events", _read_with_fake)
+
+    stream_resp = client.get(f"/stream/{posted_run_id}")
+    assert stream_resp.status_code == 200
+    assert "text/event-stream" in stream_resp.headers["content-type"]
+    events_seen = _parse_sse_block(stream_resp.text)
+    names = [e["event"] for e in events_seen]
+    assert names == ["scope_decision", "run_complete"]
+    first_event_id = events_seen[0]["id"]
+    run_complete_payload = events_seen[1]["data"]
+    assert run_complete_payload["run_id"] == posted_run_id
+    assert run_complete_payload["status"] == "success"
+
+    # ----- Step 5: GET /stream/{id} with Last-Event-ID resume -------------
+    # Per Codex iter-2 P1-003: pin the resume semantics. After consuming
+    # scope_decision, a reconnect with Last-Event-ID=<first_id> should
+    # return only run_complete (replay starts after the consumed event).
+    resume_resp = client.get(
+        f"/stream/{posted_run_id}", headers={"Last-Event-ID": first_event_id}
+    )
+    assert resume_resp.status_code == 200
+    resume_events = _parse_sse_block(resume_resp.text)
+    assert [e["event"] for e in resume_events] == ["run_complete"]
+
+    # ----- Step 6: GET /runs/{id}/bundle.tar.gz ---------------------------
+    app_with_v6_routers.dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn] = _stub_sign_fn
+    bundle_resp = client.get(f"/runs/{posted_run_id}/bundle.tar.gz")
+    # Critical I-arch-001d P1-001 regression check: signer override must fire
+    # — if Depends() callable identity is wrong, we'd see 503 gpg_unavailable.
+    assert bundle_resp.status_code != 503, (
+        f"signer override did not fire — Depends(get_sign_fn) callable "
+        f"identity mismatch. Got {bundle_resp.status_code}: {bundle_resp.text[:300]}"
+    )
+
+    # ----- Step 7: extract tar + cross-validate IDs -----------------------
+    # Per Codex iter-3 P1-006: bundle structure is
+    #   audit_<bundle_id>/{manifest.yaml, verified_report.json, ...}
+    # NOT manifest.json. Use yaml.safe_load on manifest.yaml.
+    if bundle_resp.status_code == 200:
+        assert "application/gzip" in bundle_resp.headers.get("content-type", "")
+        with tarfile.open(fileobj=io.BytesIO(bundle_resp.content), mode="r:gz") as tar:
+            names = tar.getnames()
+            assert len(names) > 0, "empty tar"
+            bundle_dir = names[0].split("/")[0]
+            manifest_member = tar.extractfile(f"{bundle_dir}/manifest.yaml")
+            assert manifest_member is not None, f"missing manifest.yaml in {names}"
+            bundle_manifest = yaml.safe_load(manifest_member.read())
+            report_member = tar.extractfile(f"{bundle_dir}/verified_report.json")
+            assert report_member is not None, f"missing verified_report.json in {names}"
+            bundle_report = json.loads(report_member.read())
+
+        # Per Codex iter-2 P2 nudge + iter-3 P2: assert the FK chain inside the bundle.
+        assert bundle_manifest["report_id"] == bundle_report["report_id"]
+        assert (
+            bundle_manifest["decision_id"]
+            == bundle_report["decision_id"]
+            == f"dec-{posted_run_id}"
+        )
+        # Per Codex iter-3 P2: pool_id (not evidence_pool_id) is the manifest field.
+        if "pool_id" in bundle_manifest:
+            assert bundle_manifest["pool_id"] == bundle_report["pool_id"]
+
+    # Per Codex iter-3 P1-006 second half: external_run_id is asserted against
+    # the SOURCE manifest.json and run_store record, NOT against bundle manifest.
+    src_after = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+    assert src_after["external_run_id"] == posted_run_id
+    record = run_store.get_run(posted_run_id, path=str(isolated_runs_db))
+    assert record is not None

 106: def _stub_sign_fn():

 114: def _parse_sse_block(raw: str) -> list[dict]:
 115:     """Parse SSE wire format into list of dicts with optional id/event/data."""
 116:     normalized = raw.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")
 117:     events: list[dict] = []
 118:     for block in normalized.split("\n\n"):
 119:         block = block.strip()
 120:         if not block:
 121:             continue
 122:         evt: dict = {}
 123:         for line in block.splitlines():
 124:             line = line.strip()
 125:             if line.startswith(":"):
 126:                 continue
 127:             if line.startswith("event:"):
 128:                 evt["event"] = line[len("event:"):].strip()
 129:             elif line.startswith("data:"):
 130:                 evt["data"] = json.loads(line[len("data:"):].strip())
 131:             elif line.startswith("id:"):
 132:                 evt["id"] = line[len("id:"):].strip()
 133:         if evt.get("event"):
 134:             events.append(evt)
 135:     return events

 143: def test_e2e_post_run_through_stream_resume_and_bundle(
 144:     app_with_v6_routers,
 145:     isolated_runs_db,
 146:     fake_server,
 147:     sync_fake,
 148:     async_fake,
 149:     tmp_path,
 150:     monkeypatch,
 151: ):
 152:     """Capstone test pinning POST/runs → stream → resume → bundle chain."""
 153:     from fastapi.testclient import TestClient
 154: 
 155:     client = TestClient(app_with_v6_routers)
 156: 
 157:     # ----- Step 1: POST /runs ---------------------------------------------
 158:     create_resp = client.post(
 159:         "/runs", json={"template": "clinical", "question": "synthetic question"}
 160:     )
 161:     assert create_resp.status_code == 202, create_resp.text
 162:     create_body = create_resp.json()
 163:     posted_run_id = create_body["run_id"]
 164:     assert create_body["lifecycle_status"] == "queued"
 165: 
 166:     # ----- Step 2: simulate pipeline-A side-effects -----------------------
 167:     # 2a. Build a synthetic AuditIR-shape artifact directory.
 168:     artifact_dir = _write_synthetic_artifact_dir(tmp_path)
 169: 
 170:     # 2b. Patch the source manifest.json to thread the POST uuid + decision_id
 171:     #     consistently — per Codex iter-2 P1-001. The augment_v6_manifest helper
 172:     #     would normally do this inside pipeline-A; in the test we set the
 173:     #     final values directly so artifact_to_slice_chain produces a
 174:     #     ScopeDecision with our decision_id.
 175:     manifest_path = artifact_dir / "manifest.json"
 176:     src_manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 177:     src_manifest["external_run_id"] = posted_run_id
 178:     src_manifest["scope"]["decision_id"] = f"dec-{posted_run_id}"
 179:     src_manifest["slug"] = "synthetic_e2e"
 180:     manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(src_manifest, sort_keys=True), encoding="utf-8")
 181: 
 182:     # 2c. run_store transitions (the Phase-0 actor stub does NOT call these;
 183:     #     the real pipeline-A actor will).
 184:     run_store.mark_in_progress(posted_run_id, path=str(isolated_runs_db))
 185:     run_store.set_pipeline_meta(
 186:         posted_run_id,
 187:         query_slug="synthetic_e2e",
 188:         artifact_dir=str(artifact_dir),
 189:         manifest_run_id=src_manifest["run_id"],
 190:         decision_id=f"dec-{posted_run_id}",
 191:         path=str(isolated_runs_db),
 192:     )
 193:     # 2d. Emit pipeline-A events into fakeredis.
 194:     _run_events_module.emit_event(
 195:         posted_run_id,
 196:         "scope_gate.completed",
 197:         {"decision": "in_scope", "reason": "synthetic"},
 198:         redis_client=sync_fake,
 199:     )
 200:     _run_events_module.emit_terminal_event(
 201:         posted_run_id, "success", redis_client=sync_fake,
 202:     )
 203:     # 2e. Final run_store transition.
 204:     run_store.mark_completed(
 205:         posted_run_id,
 206:         {"manifest": {"status": "success"}, "status": "success"},
 207:         pipeline_status="success",
 208:         cost_usd=0.42,
 209:         path=str(isolated_runs_db),
 210:     )
 211: 
 212:     # ----- Step 3: GET /runs/{id} -----------------------------------------
 213:     get_resp = client.get(f"/runs/{posted_run_id}")
 214:     assert get_resp.status_code == 200, get_resp.text
 215:     get_body = get_resp.json()
 216:     assert get_body["lifecycle_status"] == "completed"
 217:     assert get_body["pipeline_status"] == "success"
 218: 
 219:     # ----- Step 4: GET /stream/{id} ---------------------------------------
 220:     # Monkeypatch stream module's read_events to feed pre-seeded fakeredis to
 221:     # the async reader (same pattern as I-arch-001e tests).
 222:     from polaris_v6.api import stream as stream_module
 223:     real_read = _run_events_module.read_events
 224: 
 225:     async def _read_with_fake(run_id, last_event_id="0-0", *, block_ms=5000, redis_client_async=None):
 226:         async for sid, raw in real_read(

  28: async def _redis_stream_source(
  29:     run_id: str, last_event_id: str, *, redis_client_async=None
  30: ) -> AsyncIterator[dict]:
  31:     """Yield SSE event dicts sourced from the Redis Stream for this run_id.
  32: 
  33:     Each yielded event includes `id: <stream_id>` so the EventSource client
  34:     resumes via Last-Event-ID on reconnect. Empty XREAD windows yield a
  35:     keepalive comment frame. Terminates after a v6 `run_complete`.
  36:     """
  37:     async for stream_id, raw_event in read_events(
  38:         run_id,
  39:         last_event_id=last_event_id,
  40:         redis_client_async=redis_client_async,
  41:     ):
  42:         if stream_id == "__keepalive__":
  43:             yield {"comment": "keepalive"}
  44:             continue
  45:         v6 = translate(raw_event)
  46:         if v6 is None:
  47:             continue

  50:             "id": stream_id,
  51:             "event": v6_name,
  52:             "data": json.dumps({"run_id": run_id, **v6_payload}),
  53:         }
  54:         if v6_name == "run_complete":
  55:             return

   1: """I-arch-001e — durable replayable SSE event log via Redis Streams.

   3: Pipeline-A emits stage events via sync `emit_event()` (non-raising). The SSE

  20: logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
  21: 
  22: EVENT_STREAM_KEY = "polaris:events:{run_id}"
  23: _LAST_EVENT_ID_RE = re.compile(r"^\d+-\d+$")
  24: DEFAULT_REDIS_URL = "redis://localhost:6379/0"

  40: 
  41:     Bad input → fall back to "0-0" (read from beginning). Caller can supply
  42:     None or empty string to mean same thing.

  49: def emit_event(

  52:     payload: dict[str, Any],

  56:     """Best-effort, non-raising XADD to `polaris:events:{run_id}`.

  88: def emit_terminal_event(
  89:     external_run_id: str | None,
  90:     pipeline_status: str,
  91:     error_msg: str | None = None,
  92:     *,
  93:     redis_client=None,
  94: ) -> None:
  95:     """Single helper for the 7 pipeline-A exit paths.
  96: 
  97:     Emits a `run.completed` event that the translator maps to v6 `run_complete`
  98:     with payload.status carrying the original pipeline_status (success /
  99:     partial_* / abort_* / error_unexpected / stream_lost).
 100:     """
 101:     payload: dict[str, Any] = {"status": pipeline_status}
 102:     if error_msg:
 103:         payload["error"] = error_msg
 104:     emit_event(external_run_id, "run.completed", payload, redis_client=redis_client)
 105: 
 106: 
 107: # Translator: pipeline-A event_type → (v6_event_name, transform_fn).
 108: # All terminal pipeline-A events (run.completed/aborted/failed) collapse to v6
 109: # `run_complete` carrying the original status.
 110: _TRANSLATOR: dict[str, tuple[str, Any]] = {
 111:     "scope_gate.completed": ("scope_decision", lambda p: {
 112:         "verdict": p.get("decision", "unknown"),
 113:         "reason": p.get("reason", ""),
 114:     }),
 115:     "corpus_adequacy.completed": ("retrieval_progress", lambda p: {
 116:         "sources_found": p.get("pool_size", 0),
 117:         "tier_breakdown": p.get("tier_counts", {}),
 118:     }),
 119:     "evidence.id_assigned": ("evidence_id", lambda p: {
 120:         "evidence_id": p.get("id", ""),
 121:         "source_url": p.get("url", ""),
 122:     }),
 123:     "strict_verify.section_completed": ("verifier_verdict", lambda p: {
 124:         "section": p.get("section", ""),
 125:         "local_pass": p.get("local", False),
 126:         "global_pass": p.get("global", False),
 127:     }),
 128:     "generator.section_completed": ("section_complete", lambda p: {
 129:         "section": p.get("section", ""),
 130:         "verified_sentences": p.get("verified", 0),
 131:         "dropped": p.get("dropped", 0),
 132:     }),
 133:     "run.completed": ("run_complete", lambda p: dict(p)),  # passthrough
 134: }
 135: 
 136: 
 137: def translate(pipeline_event: dict[str, Any]) -> tuple[str, dict[str, Any]] | None:
 138:     """Translate a pipeline-A event payload to v6 (name, payload) or None."""
 139:     event_type = pipeline_event.get("event_type")
 140:     mapping = _TRANSLATOR.get(event_type or "")
 141:     if mapping is None:
 142:         return None
 143:     v6_name, payload_fn = mapping
 144:     try:
 145:         payload = json.loads(pipeline_event.get("payload", "{}"))
 146:     except json.JSONDecodeError:
 147:         payload = {}
 148:     return v6_name, payload_fn(payload)
 149: 
 150: 
 151: # Grace period (seconds) after run_store reports lifecycle_status terminal but
 152: # no Redis terminal event has been seen. After this elapses, emit a synthetic
 153: # `run_complete(status=stream_lost)` so the client gets a deterministic close
 154: # rather than hanging on keepalives forever. Per Codex iter-2 P1-3 + diff iter-1.
 155: STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS = 10.0
 156: 
 157: 
 158: def _get_lifecycle_status(external_run_id: str) -> str | None:
 159:     """Best-effort sync run_store lookup. Returns lifecycle_status or None.
 160: 
 161:     Imported lazily so tests that don't touch run_store don't pay sqlite init.
 162:     Any failure (missing DB, import error, schema drift) returns None so the
 163:     reader keeps emitting keepalives rather than synthesizing a stream_lost
 164:     terminal on transient backend hiccups.
 165:     """
 166:     try:
 167:         from polaris_v6.queue import run_store  # noqa: PLC0415
 168: 
 169:         row = run_store.get_run(external_run_id)
 170:         if row is None:
 171:             return None
 172:         return getattr(row, "lifecycle_status", None)
 173:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — observability lookup never blocks SSE
 174:         logger.warning(
 175:             "[run_events] run_store lookup failed run_id=%s: %s",
 176:             external_run_id,
 177:             exc,
 178:         )
 179:         return None
 180: 
 181: 
 182: async def _check_lifecycle_terminal(external_run_id: str) -> bool:
 183:     """Async wrapper for the sync sqlite lookup."""
 184:     import asyncio  # noqa: PLC0415
 185:     status = await asyncio.to_thread(_get_lifecycle_status, external_run_id)
 186:     return status in ("completed", "failed")
 187: 
 188: 
 189: def _is_connection_failure(exc: BaseException) -> bool:
 190:     """Narrow stream_unavailable to actual Redis reachability failures.
 191: 
 192:     Per Codex diff iter-1 P1: every XREAD exception was being mapped to
 193:     stream_unavailable, masking schema bugs / corrupt entries as 'Redis down'.
 194:     Now we treat ONLY connection/timeout/socket failures as unavailability;
 195:     other exceptions surface as stream_lost.
 196:     """
 197:     if isinstance(exc, (ConnectionError, TimeoutError, OSError)):
 198:         return True
 199:     # redis.asyncio raises ConnectionError subclasses; check by class name
 200:     # to avoid a hard import dependency.
 201:     name = type(exc).__name__
 202:     return name in {
 203:         "ConnectionError",
 204:         "TimeoutError",
 205:         "BusyLoadingError",
 206:         "ConnectionResetError",
 207:         "RedisConnectionError",
 208:     }
 209: 
 210: 
 211: async def read_events(
 212:     external_run_id: str,
 213:     last_event_id: str = "0-0",
 214:     *,
 215:     block_ms: int = 5000,
 216:     redis_client_async=None,
 217: ) -> AsyncIterator[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]:
 218:     """Async generator yielding (stream_id, raw_pipeline_event_dict).
 219: 
 220:     Terminates after emitting a `run.completed` event. Per Codex iter-2 P1-3
 221:     + diff iter-1 P1:
 222: 
 223:     - empty XREAD window → keepalive (caller emits SSE comment frame), then
 224:       check run_store. While lifecycle_status is queued/in_progress, keep
 225:       emitting keepalives.
 226:     - lifecycle_status in {completed, failed} AND no terminal event seen in
 227:       the next STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS → emit a synthetic
 228:       run_complete(status=stream_lost) and close cleanly.
 229:     - actual Redis connection/timeout failure → emit
 230:       run_complete(status=stream_unavailable) and close.
 231:     - non-reachability XREAD exception → emit stream_lost and close (treat as
 232:       degraded stream rather than 'Redis down').
 233:     """
 234:     import asyncio  # noqa: PLC0415
 235: 
 236:     last_id = _validate_last_event_id(last_event_id)
 237:     key = EVENT_STREAM_KEY.format(run_id=external_run_id)
 238: 
 239:     try:
 240:         if redis_client_async is None:
 241:             import redis.asyncio as aredis  # noqa: PLC0415
 242:             client = aredis.from_url(_redis_url(), decode_responses=False)
 243:         else:
 244:             client = redis_client_async
 245:     except ImportError:
 246:         yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_unavailable"})})
 247:         return
 248: 
 249:     # Tracks first-seen-at for lifecycle_status terminal so we can apply the
 250:     # grace window before declaring stream_lost.
 251:     lifecycle_terminal_first_seen: float | None = None
 252:     loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
 253: 
 254:     try:
 255:         while True:
 256:             try:
 257:                 events = await client.xread({key: last_id}, count=100, block=block_ms)
 258:             except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
 259:                 if _is_connection_failure(exc):
 260:                     logger.warning(
 261:                         "[run_events] redis unreachable run_id=%s: %s",
 262:                         external_run_id,
 263:                         exc,
 264:                     )
 265:                     yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_unavailable"})})
 266:                     return
 267:                 # Non-reachability failure — log and degrade to stream_lost.
 268:                 logger.warning(
 269:                     "[run_events] xread error run_id=%s: %s",
 270:                     external_run_id,
 271:                     exc,
 272:                 )
 273:                 yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_lost"})})
 274:                 return
 275: 
 276:             if not events:
 277:                 # Empty XREAD window — emit keepalive then consult run_store.
 278:                 yield ("__keepalive__", {})
 279:                 if await _check_lifecycle_terminal(external_run_id):
 280:                     now = loop.time()
 281:                     if lifecycle_terminal_first_seen is None:
 282:                         lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = now
 283:                     elif now - lifecycle_terminal_first_seen >= STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS:
 284:                         logger.warning(
 285:                             "[run_events] lifecycle terminal without redis terminal "
 286:                             "run_id=%s — emitting synthetic stream_lost",
 287:                             external_run_id,
 288:                         )
 289:                         yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_lost"})})
 290:                         return
 291:                 else:
 292:                     # Reset the grace window if the run un-terminals (shouldn't happen,
 293:                     # but the lifecycle is the source of truth).
 294:                     lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = None
 295:                 continue
 296: 
 297:             # Real events arrived → reset the grace window.
 298:             lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = None
 299: 
 300:             for _stream_name, entries in events:
 301:                 for entry_id, fields in entries:
 302:                     stream_id = entry_id.decode() if isinstance(entry_id, bytes) else entry_id
 303:                     last_id = stream_id
 304:                     event_type = fields.get(b"event_type") or fields.get("event_type")
 305:                     payload = fields.get(b"payload") or fields.get("payload")
 306:                     if isinstance(event_type, bytes):
 307:                         event_type = event_type.decode()
 308:                     if isinstance(payload, bytes):
 309:                         payload = payload.decode()
 310:                     yield (stream_id, {"event_type": event_type, "payload": payload})
 311:                     if event_type == "run.completed":
 312:                         return
 313:     finally:
 314:         # aredis client lazy-closed via context if possible
 315:         try:
 316:             close = getattr(client, "aclose", None) or getattr(client, "close", None)
 317:             if close:
 318:                 result = close()
 319:                 if hasattr(result, "__await__"):
 320:                     await result
 321:         except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — defensive close
 322:             pass

  58:     fixture_name = _GOLDEN_RUN_INDEX.get(run_id)
  59:     if fixture_name is None:
  60:         raise HTTPException(
  61:             status_code=404,
  62:             detail=f"Bundle for run {run_id!r} not found. Available golden runs: {list(_GOLDEN_RUN_INDEX)}",
  63:         )
  64:     raw = json.loads((_FIXTURE_DIR / fixture_name).read_text())
  65:     return EvidenceContract.model_validate(raw)
  66: 
  67: 
  68: @router.get("/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz")
  69: def get_run_bundle_targz(
  70:     run_id: str,
  71:     sign_fn=Depends(get_sign_fn),
  72: ):
  73:     """Resolve run_id → artifact_dir → signed audit bundle (tar.gz).
  74: 
  75:     I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-1 P1-001: `Depends(get_sign_fn)` MUST use
  76:     the actual `get_sign_fn` callable from audit_bundle_route — the
  77:     create_app() registers `app.dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn]` to
  78:     inject the real GPGSigner when POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is set. A lambda
  79:     Depends would be a different callable; the override would never fire.
  80: 
  81:     Status codes:
  82:         200: bundleable run; returns application/gzip
  83:         404: run not found, not completed, or artifact_dir missing
  84:         422: run aborted (pipeline_status=abort_*) or sovereignty cascade
  85:              emptied the report
  86:         503: GPG signer not configured (POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID unset) — surfaced
  87:              by the inner post_audit_bundle when sign_fn is None.
  88:     """
  89:     info = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  90:     if info is None:
  91:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail={"error": "run not found"})
  92:     if info.lifecycle_status != "completed":
  93:         raise HTTPException(
  94:             status_code=404,
  95:             detail={"error": f"run not completed: lifecycle_status={info.lifecycle_status}"},
  96:         )
  97:     if info.pipeline_status and info.pipeline_status.startswith("abort_"):
  98:         raise HTTPException(
  99:             status_code=422,
 100:             detail={"error": f"run aborted: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status}", "bundleable": False},
 101:         )
 102:     if not info.artifact_dir:
 103:         raise HTTPException(
 104:             status_code=404, detail={"error": "run has no artifact_dir recorded"}
 105:         )
 106: 
 107:     artifact_dir = Path(info.artifact_dir)
 108:     if not artifact_dir.is_dir():
 109:         raise HTTPException(
 110:             status_code=404,
 111:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir does not exist on disk: {artifact_dir}"},
 112:         )
 113: 
 114:     # I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-2 P1-002 fix: release_allowed gate.
 115:     # The slice-chain pipeline_verdict collapses partial_* into "success",
 116:     # but a release-blocked partial (e.g. partial_qwen_advisory with
 117:     # release_allowed=false) MUST NOT ship as a clean bundle. Read the raw
 118:     # manifest.release_allowed flag and refuse with 422 when False.
 119:     try:
 120:         manifest_raw = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 121:     except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError) as exc:
 122:         raise HTTPException(
 123:             status_code=404,
 124:             detail={"error": f"manifest.json missing or invalid: {exc}"},
 125:         ) from exc
 126:     if not manifest_raw.get("release_allowed", False):
 127:         raise HTTPException(
 128:             status_code=422,
 129:             detail={
 130:                 "error": (
 131:                     f"run release-blocked: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status!r}, "
 132:                     f"release_allowed=False. Bundle cannot ship until release gate clears."
 133:                 ),
 134:                 "bundleable": False,
 135:                 "pipeline_status": info.pipeline_status,
 136:             },
 137:         )
 138: 
 139:     try:
 140:         decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
 141:     except SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError as exc:
 142:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail={"error": str(exc)}) from exc
 143:     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
 144:         raise HTTPException(
 145:             status_code=404,
 146:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir incomplete: {exc}"},
 147:         ) from exc
 148: 
 149:     return post_audit_bundle(
 150:         AuditBundleRequest(decision=decision, pool=pool, report=report),
 151:         sign_fn=sign_fn,
 152:     )

  13: 
  14: from __future__ import annotations
  15: 
  16: import json
  17: import os
  18: import sqlite3
  19: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  20: from typing import Any
  21: 
  22: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  23: 
  24: DEFAULT_DB_PATH = "state/v6_runs.sqlite"
  25: ENV_DB_PATH = "POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB"
  26: 
  27: 
  28: def _resolve_path(path: str | None) -> str:
  29:     if path is not None:
  30:         return path
  31:     return os.environ.get(ENV_DB_PATH, DEFAULT_DB_PATH)
  32: 
  33: 
  34: def _now_iso() -> str:
  35:     return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  36: 
  37: 
  38: def _connect(path: str | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
  39:     resolved = _resolve_path(path)
  40:     parent = os.path.dirname(resolved)
  41:     if parent:
  42:         os.makedirs(parent, exist_ok=True)
  43:     conn = sqlite3.connect(resolved)
  44:     conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
  45:     return conn
  46: 
  47: 
  48: def _migrate_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
  49:     """Idempotent additive migration. Safe to call on every init_db.
  50: 
  51:     1. Create base table if absent.
  52:     2. If legacy `status` column exists and `lifecycle_status` doesn't,
  53:        RENAME COLUMN to preserve values (SQLite 3.25+, Python 3.11 ships
  54:        SQLite 3.34+).
  55:     3. ADD COLUMN for each I-arch-001a field if missing.
  56:     4. CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS for query lookups.
  57:     """
  58:     conn.execute(
  59:         """
  60:         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS runs (
  61:             run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  62:             template TEXT NOT NULL,
  63:             question TEXT NOT NULL,
  64:             lifecycle_status TEXT NOT NULL,
  65:             queued_at TEXT NOT NULL,
  66:             started_at TEXT,
  67:             finished_at TEXT,
  68:             result_json TEXT,
  69:             error_json TEXT
  70:         )
  71:         """
  72:     )
  73:     cols = {row[1] for row in conn.execute("PRAGMA table_info(runs)").fetchall()}
  74:     if "status" in cols and "lifecycle_status" not in cols:
  75:         conn.execute("ALTER TABLE runs RENAME COLUMN status TO lifecycle_status")
  76:         cols.discard("status")
  77:         cols.add("lifecycle_status")
  78:     for col_name, col_type in {
  79:         "query_slug": "TEXT",
  80:         "manifest_run_id": "TEXT",
  81:         "artifact_dir": "TEXT",
  82:         "pipeline_status": "TEXT",
  83:         "cost_usd": "REAL",
  84:         "decision_id": "TEXT",
  85:     }.items():
  86:         if col_name not in cols:
  87:             conn.execute(f"ALTER TABLE runs ADD COLUMN {col_name} {col_type}")
  88:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_query_slug ON runs(query_slug)")
  89:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_manifest_run_id ON runs(manifest_run_id)")
  90: 
  91: 
  92: def init_db(path: str | None = None) -> None:
  93:     """Create the runs table if absent, run migrations. Idempotent."""
  94:     conn = _connect(path)
  95:     try:
  96:         conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
  97:         _migrate_schema(conn)
  98:         conn.commit()
  99:     finally:
 100:         conn.close()

 230: def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 231:     """Return the run record or None if missing.
 232: 
 233:     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
 234:     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
 235:     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
 236:     contract.
 237: 
 238:     I-arch-001a Codex iter-2 P2-002: if a known DB exists with the legacy
 239:     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.
 240:     The defensive catch below detects "no such column" and triggers a
 241:     one-time migration via init_db before retrying.
 242:     """
 243:     conn = _connect(path)
 244:     try:
 245:         try:
 246:             row = conn.execute(
 247:                 "SELECT run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
 248:                 "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
 249:                 "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id "
 250:                 "FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 251:                 (run_id,),
 252:             ).fetchone()
 253:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 254:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 255:             # Narrow per Codex iter-1 P2-001: only the missing-table stub
 256:             # path returns None; surface other operational errors (schema
 257:             # corruption, migration faults) so they aren't masked as
 258:             # missing-row.
 259:             if "no such table" in msg:
 260:                 return None
 261:             # Codex iter-2 P2-002: legacy schema → migrate then retry once.
 262:             if "no such column" in msg:
 263:                 conn.close()
 264:                 init_db(path)
 265:                 conn = _connect(path)
 266:                 row = conn.execute(
 267:                     "SELECT run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
 268:                     "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
 269:                     "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id "
 270:                     "FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 271:                     (run_id,),
 272:                 ).fetchone()
 273:             else:
 274:                 raise
 275:     finally:
 276:         conn.close()
 277:     if row is None:
 278:         return None
 279:     return RunStatusResponse(
 280:         run_id=row["run_id"],
 281:         template=row["template"],
 282:         question=row["question"],
 283:         lifecycle_status=row["lifecycle_status"],
 284:         pipeline_status=row["pipeline_status"],
 285:         queued_at=row["queued_at"],

 107: 
 108:     # Verification details — sections list with kept[] / dropped[] keys per loader._parse_verified_report.
 109:     sections = []
 110:     for sec_idx, title in enumerate(titles):
 111:         kept_sentences = []
 112:         for i in range(sentences_per_section):

 114:                 cited_evidence_ids_per_sentence[sec_idx * sentences_per_section + i]
 115:                 if cited_evidence_ids_per_sentence

 118:             tokens = [{"evidence_id": eid, "start": 0, "end": 100} for eid in cited_ids]
 119:             kept_sentences.append({
 120:                 "sentence": f"Synthetic sentence {i} in {title}.",
 121:                 "tokens": tokens,
 122:                 "failure_reasons": [],
 123:             })
 124:         sections.append({
 125:             "title": title,
 126:             "kept": kept_sentences,
 127:             "dropped": [],
 128:             "total_kept": sentences_per_section,
 129:             "total_dropped": 0,
 130:             "total_in": sentences_per_section,

 132:         })

 135:         "totals": {

 164:         path=str(isolated_db),

 167:         "run_signed",
 168:         {"manifest": {"status": "success"}, "status": "success"},

 175:     def _stub_sign_fn():
 176:         def _sign(_data: bytes) -> bytes:
 177:             return b"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\nstub\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n"
 178:         return _sign

 180:     app_with_bundle_router.dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn] = _stub_sign_fn
 181:     client = TestClient(app_with_bundle_router)
 182:     resp = client.get("/runs/run_signed/bundle.tar.gz")
 183:     # P1-001 regression: with override, the endpoint must reach the signer and
 184:     # NOT short-circuit on 503. We accept either 200 (signed tar.gz returned)
 185:     # OR a 4xx/5xx that's NOT 503 (since the signer fired but downstream may

 187:     # validation may notice the synthetic decision_id ≠ pool.decision_id).

 191:         f"Got status {resp.status_code}, body: {resp.text[:300]}"

 succeeded in 1059ms:
   1: """FastAPI route for slice 004 audit-bundle export.
   2: 
   3: POST /api/audit-bundle — accepts a {decision, pool, report} triple
   4: (typically the slice 001 + 002 + 003 chain output) and streams back
   5: a GPG-signed audit_<bundle_id>.tar.gz file.
   6: 
   7: Mounted alongside the other slice routes in polaris_v6.api.app.
   8: """
   9: 
  10: from __future__ import annotations
  11: 
  12: import tempfile
  13: from pathlib import Path
  14: from typing import Any, Callable
  15: 
  16: from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
  17: from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
  18: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
  19: 
  20: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.bundle_builder import (
  21:     SignFn,
  22:     build_audit_bundle,
  23: )
  24: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.bundle_schema import ContentType
  25: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.manifest_builder import build_manifest_and_files
  26: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import VerifiedReport
  27: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  28: from polaris_graph.scope.scope_decision import ScopeDecision
  29: 
  30: PREVIEW_CONTENT_TYPES: tuple[ContentType, ...] = (
  31:     "scope_decision",
  32:     "evidence_pool",
  33:     "verified_report",
  34:     "source_snapshot",
  35:     "metadata",
  36: )
  37: 
  38: router = APIRouter(tags=["audit-bundle"])
  39: 
  40: 
  41: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  42: # Dependencies
  43: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  44: 
  45: def get_sign_fn() -> SignFn | None:
  46:     """Returns the active GPG signer or None.
  47: 
  48:     None signals the orchestrator's sentinel default which raises and is
  49:     caught by the route -> HTTP 503. Tests override this dep; production
  50:     binds to a real GPGSigner via app.dependency_overrides at startup
  51:     when POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is set.
  52:     """
  53:     return None
  54: 
  55: 
  56: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  57: # Request / response models
  58: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  59: 
  60: class AuditBundleRequest(BaseModel):
  61:     """POST body for /api/audit-bundle.
  62: 
  63:     Carries the full research chain (decision + pool + report). The route
  64:     re-validates the FK chain consistency before building.
  65:     """
  66: 
  67:     decision: ScopeDecision = Field(description="slice 001 ScopeDecision")
  68:     pool: EvidencePool = Field(description="slice 002 EvidencePool")
  69:     report: VerifiedReport = Field(
  70:         description="slice 003 VerifiedReport (verdict=success required)"
  71:     )
  72: 
  73: 
  74: class AuditBundleErrorResponse(BaseModel):
  75:     """Body returned with HTTP 4xx/5xx when bundle cannot be assembled."""
  76: 
  77:     error: bool = True
  78:     code: str  # 'fk_chain_mismatch' | 'verdict_not_success' |
  79:                # 'cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot' |
  80:                # 'copyrighted_span_in_bundle' |
  81:                # 'gpg_unavailable' | 'sign_failed'
  82:     message: str
  83:     report_id: str | None = None
  84: 
  85: 
  86: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  87: # Routes
  88: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  89: 
  90: @router.post("/audit-bundle")
  91: def post_audit_bundle(
  92:     req: AuditBundleRequest,
  93:     sign_fn: SignFn | None = Depends(get_sign_fn),
  94: ) -> Any:
  95:     """Build + return a GPG-signed audit bundle as application/gzip.
  96: 
  97:     Returns the .tar.gz file as a streaming download.
  98:     """
  99:     if sign_fn is None:
 100:         raise HTTPException(
 101:             status_code=503,
 102:             detail={
 103:                 "error": True,
 104:                 "code": "gpg_unavailable",
 105:                 "message": (
 106:                     "GPG signer not configured. Set POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID in env "
 107:                     "and ensure the corresponding key is in the gpg keyring."
 108:                 ),
 109:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 110:             },
 111:         )
 112: 
 113:     # Build into a temp dir; FileResponse copies it to the wire.
 114:     tmp_dir = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="polaris_audit_"))
 115:     try:
 116:         bundle_path = build_audit_bundle(
 117:             req.decision,
 118:             req.pool,
 119:             req.report,
 120:             output_dir=tmp_dir,
 121:             sign_fn=sign_fn,
 122:         )
 123:     except ValueError as exc:
 124:         # FK chain mismatch, verdict != success, cited-span unreachable, or copyrighted span
 125:         msg = str(exc)
 126:         if "copyrighted span" in msg:
 127:             code = "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 128:         elif "cited span unreachable" in msg:
 129:             code = "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 130:         elif "FK chain" in msg or "pool_id" in msg or "decision_id" in msg:
 131:             code = "fk_chain_mismatch"
 132:         else:
 133:             code = "verdict_not_success"
 134:         raise HTTPException(
 135:             status_code=400,
 136:             detail={
 137:                 "error": True,
 138:                 "code": code,
 139:                 "message": msg,
 140:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 141:             },
 142:         )
 143:     except RuntimeError as exc:
 144:         raise HTTPException(
 145:             status_code=502,
 146:             detail={
 147:                 "error": True,
 148:                 "code": "sign_failed",
 149:                 "message": str(exc),
 150:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 151:             },
 152:         )
 153: 
 154:     return FileResponse(
 155:         path=str(bundle_path),
 156:         filename=bundle_path.name,
 157:         media_type="application/gzip",
 158:     )
 159: 
 160: 
 161: @router.post("/audit-bundle/preview")
 162: def post_audit_bundle_preview(req: AuditBundleRequest) -> dict[str, Any]:
 163:     """Build the manifest only and return it for preview (no GPG, no tar)."""
 164:     if req.report.pool_id != req.pool.pool_id:
 165:         raise HTTPException(
 166:             status_code=400,
 167:             detail={
 168:                 "error": True,
 169:                 "code": "fk_chain_mismatch",
 170:                 "message": (
 171:                     f"FK chain mismatch: report.pool_id={req.report.pool_id!r}"
 172:                     f" != pool.pool_id={req.pool.pool_id!r}"
 173:                 ),
 174:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 175:             },
 176:         )
 177:     if req.report.decision_id != req.decision.decision_id:
 178:         raise HTTPException(
 179:             status_code=400,
 180:             detail={
 181:                 "error": True,
 182:                 "code": "fk_chain_mismatch",
 183:                 "message": (
 184:                     f"FK chain mismatch: report.decision_id="
 185:                     f"{req.report.decision_id!r} != decision.decision_id="
 186:                     f"{req.decision.decision_id!r}"
 187:                 ),
 188:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 189:             },
 190:         )
 191:     try:
 192:         manifest, _files_bytes = build_manifest_and_files(
 193:             req.decision, req.pool, req.report
 194:         )
 195:     except ValueError as exc:
 196:         msg = str(exc)
 197:         if "copyrighted span" in msg:
 198:             code = "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 199:         elif "cited span unreachable" in msg:
 200:             code = "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 201:         else:
 202:             code = "verdict_not_success"
 203:         raise HTTPException(
 204:             status_code=400,
 205:             detail={
 206:                 "error": True,
 207:                 "code": code,
 208:                 "message": msg,
 209:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 210:             },
 211:         )
 212:     breakdown = {ct: {"count": 0, "bytes": 0} for ct in PREVIEW_CONTENT_TYPES}
 213:     for entry in manifest.files:
 214:         slot = breakdown[entry.content_type]
 215:         slot["count"] += 1
 216:         slot["bytes"] += entry.size_bytes
 217:     return {
 218:         "preview_bundle_id": manifest.bundle_id,
 219:         "generator_model": manifest.generator_model,
 220:         "polaris_version": manifest.polaris_version,
 221:         "file_count": len(manifest.files),
 222:         "total_bytes": manifest.total_bytes(),
 223:         "content_type_breakdown": breakdown,
 224:     }

 228: def get_audit_bundle_health(
 229:     sign_fn: SignFn | None = Depends(get_sign_fn),
 230: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 231:     """Liveness probe + slice 004 backend version info.
 232: 
 233:     signing_backend reflects ACTUAL state via the Depends-injected sign_fn:

   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md` §"bundle_builder".
   4: 
   5: Pipeline:
   6:     ScopeDecision + EvidencePool + VerifiedReport (verdict=success)
   7:         ↓
   8:     build_manifest_and_files()  -> manifest + content files
   9:         ↓
  10:     serialize_manifest_yaml()    -> manifest.yaml bytes
  11:         ↓
  12:     sign_fn(manifest.yaml)       -> manifest.yaml.asc bytes
  13:         ↓
  14:     pack_tarball()               -> audit_<bundle_id>.tar.gz
  15: 
  16: The output tarball:
  17:     audit_<bundle_id>/
  18:       manifest.yaml
  19:       manifest.yaml.asc
  20:       scope_decision.json
  21:       evidence_pool.json
  22:       verified_report.json
  23:       sources/<source_id>.txt   (for each cited source)
  24:       metadata.json
  25: 
  26: External verifiers run:
  27:     tar -xzf audit_<id>.tar.gz
  28:     cd audit_<id>
  29:     gpg --verify manifest.yaml.asc manifest.yaml
  30:     # then re-hash each content file and compare against manifest.files[*].sha256
  31: """
  32: 
  33: from __future__ import annotations
  34: 
  35: import io
  36: import logging
  37: import tarfile
  38: import time
  39: from pathlib import Path
  40: from typing import Callable
  41: 
  42: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.bundle_schema import BundleManifest
  43: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.manifest_builder import (
  44:     build_manifest_and_files,
  45:     serialize_manifest_yaml,
  46: )
  47: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import VerifiedReport
  48: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  49: from polaris_graph.scope.scope_decision import ScopeDecision
  50: 
  51: _LOG = logging.getLogger(__name__)
  52: 
  53: 
  54: # Type alias for the sign function we accept (Protocol-style duck typing).
  55: # Concrete impl is GPGSigner from gpg_signer.py; tests can pass a stub.
  56: SignFn = Callable[[bytes], bytes]
  57: 
  58: 
  59: def _default_sign_fn(_payload: bytes) -> bytes:
  60:     """Sentinel that refuses to run.
  61: 
  62:     Forces callers to provide a real signer (or test stub). Per LAW II,
  63:     silently writing an unsigned bundle is FORBIDDEN — the audit bundle's
  64:     legal value comes from the signature.
  65:     """
  66:     raise NotImplementedError(
  67:         "no sign_fn injected. The audit bundle MUST be GPG-signed. "
  68:         "Inject a real signer (e.g. GPGSigner from gpg_signer.py) or "
  69:         "a test stub."
  70:     )
  71: 
  72: 
  73: def build_audit_bundle(
  74:     decision: ScopeDecision,
  75:     pool: EvidencePool,
  76:     report: VerifiedReport,
  77:     output_dir: Path,
  78:     sign_fn: SignFn = _default_sign_fn,
  79: ) -> Path:
  80:     """End-to-end: build manifest + sign + pack tarball.
  81: 
  82:     Args:
  83:         decision: slice 001 ScopeDecision
  84:         pool: slice 002 EvidencePool (must match report.pool_id)
  85:         report: slice 003 VerifiedReport (must have verdict=success)
  86:         output_dir: directory where audit_<id>.tar.gz is written
  87:         sign_fn: function that takes manifest.yaml bytes and returns
  88:                  .asc bytes. Default raises NotImplementedError; callers
  89:                  MUST inject a real signer.
  90: 
  91:     Returns:
  92:         Path to the generated audit_<bundle_id>.tar.gz file.
  93: 
  94:     Raises:
  95:         ValueError: if report.pipeline_verdict != 'success' or pool/report
  96:                     FK chain inconsistent.
  97:         RuntimeError: if sign_fn raises (propagated, original error chained).
  98:     """
  99:     if report.pool_id != pool.pool_id:
 100:         raise ValueError(
 101:             f"FK chain mismatch: report.pool_id={report.pool_id!r} != "
 102:             f"pool.pool_id={pool.pool_id!r}"
 103:         )
 104:     if report.decision_id != decision.decision_id:
 105:         raise ValueError(
 106:             f"FK chain mismatch: report.decision_id={report.decision_id!r}"
 107:             f" != decision.decision_id={decision.decision_id!r}"
 108:         )
 109: 
 110:     t_start = time.perf_counter()
 111:     manifest, content_files = build_manifest_and_files(decision, pool, report)
 112: 
 113:     manifest_yaml = serialize_manifest_yaml(manifest)
 114: 
 115:     try:
 116:         manifest_sig = sign_fn(manifest_yaml)
 117:     except NotImplementedError:
 118:         raise RuntimeError(
 119:             "audit bundle requires a sign_fn; default sentinel forbids "
 120:             "shipping unsigned bundles per CLAUDE.md LAW II"
 121:         )
 122:     except Exception as exc:
 123:         raise RuntimeError(
 124:             f"sign_fn raised {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
 125:         ) from exc
 126: 
 127:     # Pack everything into a single .tar.gz under top-level dir audit_<id>
 128:     output_dir = Path(output_dir)
 129:     output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 130:     bundle_filename = f"audit_{manifest.bundle_id}.tar.gz"
 131:     bundle_path = output_dir / bundle_filename
 132: 
 133:     with tarfile.open(bundle_path, "w:gz") as tar:
 134:         top_dir = f"audit_{manifest.bundle_id}"
 135: 
 136:         # 1. manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc (NOT in manifest.files;
 137:         #    they are the manifest itself + signature)
 138:         _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/manifest.yaml", manifest_yaml)
 139:         _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/manifest.yaml.asc", manifest_sig)
 140: 
 141:         # 2. Content files (paths from manifest.files)
 142:         for path, content_bytes in content_files.items():
 143:             _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/{path}", content_bytes)
 144: 
 145:     elapsed_ms = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 146:     _LOG.info(
 147:         "audit bundle built bundle_id=%s files=%d size=%dB elapsed=%dms",
 148:         manifest.bundle_id,
 149:         len(manifest.files),
 150:         bundle_path.stat().st_size,
 151:         elapsed_ms,
 152:     )
 153:     return bundle_path
 154: 
 155: 
 156: def _add_file(tar: tarfile.TarFile, name: str, data: bytes) -> None:
 157:     """Add bytes to a tarfile under `name`."""
 158:     info = tarfile.TarInfo(name=name)
 159:     info.size = len(data)
 160:     info.mtime = int(time.time())
 161:     info.mode = 0o644
 162:     tar.addfile(info, io.BytesIO(data))
 163: 
 164: 
 165: def extract_manifest_from_bundle(
 166:     bundle_path: Path,
 167: ) -> tuple[BundleManifest, bytes, bytes]:
 168:     """Helper for verifiers/tests: extract manifest + signature + their bytes.
 169: 
 170:     Returns:
 171:         (manifest, manifest_yaml_bytes, manifest_sig_bytes)
 172: 
 173:     Raises FileNotFoundError if either is missing in the tarball.
 174:     """
 175:     bundle_path = Path(bundle_path)
 176:     manifest_yaml: bytes | None = None
 177:     manifest_sig: bytes | None = None
 178: 
 179:     with tarfile.open(bundle_path, "r:gz") as tar:
 180:         for member in tar.getmembers():
 181:             if member.name.endswith("manifest.yaml") and not member.name.endswith(
 182:                 "manifest.yaml.asc"
 183:             ):
 184:                 f = tar.extractfile(member)
 185:                 if f is not None:
 186:                     manifest_yaml = f.read()
 187:             elif member.name.endswith("manifest.yaml.asc"):
 188:                 f = tar.extractfile(member)
 189:                 if f is not None:
 190:                     manifest_sig = f.read()
 191: 
 192:     if manifest_yaml is None:
 193:         raise FileNotFoundError(
 194:             f"manifest.yaml not found in bundle {bundle_path}"
 195:         )
 196:     if manifest_sig is None:
 197:         raise FileNotFoundError(
 198:             f"manifest.yaml.asc not found in bundle {bundle_path}"
 199:         )
 200: 
 201:     import yaml
 202: 
 203:     parsed = yaml.safe_load(manifest_yaml.decode("utf-8"))
 204:     manifest = BundleManifest.model_validate(parsed)
 205:     return manifest, manifest_yaml, manifest_sig

   1: """Manifest builder — collects all bundle content + computes SHA256s.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md` §"manifest_builder".
   4: 
   5: Given a ScopeDecision + EvidencePool + VerifiedReport (the research chain
   6: output), serializes each to canonical JSON, snapshots cited source
   7: texts, and assembles a BundleManifest with SHA256 anchors over every
   8: content file.

  12: the signature.
  13: """

  16:

  18: import json
  19: from datetime import datetime, timezone

  23:

  56: def _sha256_bytes(data: bytes) -> str:
  57:     return hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest()
  58: 
  59: 
  60: def _serialize_json_canonical(model: Any) -> bytes:
  61:     """Pydantic model -> deterministic UTF-8 JSON bytes.
  62: 
  63:     sort_keys + no extra whitespace beyond standard separators ensures
  64:     re-serialization on the verifier side produces identical bytes →
  65:     SHA256 stable across implementations.
  66:     """
  67:     if hasattr(model, "model_dump"):
  68:         payload = model.model_dump(mode="json")
  69:     else:
  70:         payload = model
  71:     return json.dumps(
  72:         payload,
  73:         sort_keys=True,
  74:         ensure_ascii=False,
  75:         separators=(",", ":"),
  76:     ).encode("utf-8")
  77: 
  78: 
  79: def _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report: VerifiedReport, snapshots: dict) -> None:
  80:     """Raise ValueError if any cited span exceeds its snapshot's reachable_chars.
  81: 
  82:     Validates the UNION of tokens parsed from `sentence.sentence_text` and
  83:     `sentence.provenance_tokens`, deduped by `token.raw`. Missing source_id =>
  84:     unreachable. Span end > reachable_chars => unreachable.
  85:     """
  86:     seen: set[str] = set()
  87:     for section in report.sections:
  88:         if section.section_status == "dropped":
  89:             continue
  90:         for sentence in section.verified_sentences:
  91:             if not sentence.verifier_pass:
  92:                 continue
  93:             tokens = list(extract_tokens(sentence.sentence_text))
  94:             for raw in sentence.provenance_tokens:
  95:                 tokens.extend(extract_tokens(raw))
  96:             for tok in tokens:
  97:                 if tok.raw in seen:
  98:                     continue
  99:                 seen.add(tok.raw)
 100:                 entry = snapshots.get(tok.source_id)
 101:                 if entry is None:
 102:                     raise ValueError(
 103:                         f"cited span unreachable after snapshot: source "
 104:                         f"{tok.source_id!r} not in snapshots (token={tok.raw!r})"
 105:                     )
 106:                 if not (0 <= tok.span_start < tok.span_end <= entry.reachable_chars):
 107:                     raise ValueError(
 108:                         f"cited span unreachable after snapshot: source "
 109:                         f"{tok.source_id!r} token={tok.raw!r} span="
 110:                         f"{tok.span_start}-{tok.span_end} reachable={entry.reachable_chars}"
 111:                     )
 112: 
 113: 
 114: def _safe_source_filename(source_id: str) -> str:
 115:     """Build a tar-safe filename from a source_id.
 116: 
 117:     source_id is opaque (uuid by default, but could be 'src-1' etc). We
 118:     sanitize aggressively: only [a-zA-Z0-9_-]. Anything else becomes _.
 119:     Length-capped at 100 chars to avoid pathological inputs.
 120:     """
 121:     safe = "".join(
 122:         c if c.isalnum() or c in "-_" else "_" for c in source_id
 123:     )[:100]
 124:     return f"{SOURCES_DIR}/{safe}.txt"
 125: 
 126: 
 127: def build_manifest_and_files(
 128:     decision: ScopeDecision,
 129:     pool: EvidencePool,
 130:     report: VerifiedReport,
 131: ) -> tuple[BundleManifest, dict[str, bytes]]:
 132:     """Build the bundle manifest + content-file dict.
 133: 
 134:     Returns:
 135:         (manifest, files) where files is {path: content_bytes}. The
 136:         caller (bundle_builder) packs files into a tarball and writes
 137:         the manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc alongside.
 138: 
 139:     Raises:
 140:         ValueError if report.pipeline_verdict != 'success'.
 141:     """
 142:     if report.pipeline_verdict != "success":
 143:         raise ValueError(
 144:             f"cannot build audit bundle for verdict "
 145:             f"{report.pipeline_verdict!r}; report must be successful"
 146:         )
 147: 
 148:     files_bytes: dict[str, bytes] = {}
 149: 
 150:     # 1. Slice 001 ScopeDecision
 151:     sd_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(decision)
 152:     files_bytes[FILE_SCOPE_DECISION] = sd_bytes
 153: 
 154:     # 2. Slice 002 EvidencePool
 155:     ep_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(pool)
 156:     files_bytes[FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL] = ep_bytes
 157: 
 158:     # 3. Slice 003 VerifiedReport
 159:     vr_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(report)
 160:     files_bytes[FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT] = vr_bytes
 161: 
 162:     # 4. Sovereignty: refuse to ship verbatim spans for non-cleared sources
 163:     assert_all_pool_sources_legal_cleared(pool)
 164: 
 165:     # 4b. Per-source snapshots + cited-span reachability guard
 166:     snapshot_entries = snapshot_sources_with_reachable(report, pool)
 167:     _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report, snapshot_entries)
 168:     for source_id, entry in snapshot_entries.items():
 169:         files_bytes[_safe_source_filename(source_id)] = entry.text.encode("utf-8")
 170:     snapshots = {sid: e.text for sid, e in snapshot_entries.items()}
 171: 
 172:     # 4b. REVIEWER_README ships verbatim in every bundle as metadata content_type.
 173:     readme_path = Path(__file__).parent / "REVIEWER_README.md"
 174:     files_bytes[FILE_REVIEWER_README] = readme_path.read_bytes()
 175: 
 176:     # 5. Bundle metadata (versions + creation timestamp)
 177:     metadata = {
 178:         "bundle_version": BUNDLE_VERSION,
 179:         "polaris_version": POLARIS_VERSION,
 180:         "created_at_utc": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat().replace(
 181:             "+00:00", "Z"
 182:         ),
 183:         "generator_model": report.generator_model,
 184:         "decision_id": decision.decision_id,
 185:         "pool_id": report.pool_id,
 186:         "report_id": report.report_id,
 187:         "source_snapshot_count": len(snapshots),
 188:     }
 189:     files_bytes[FILE_METADATA] = json.dumps(
 190:         metadata,
 191:         sort_keys=True,
 192:         ensure_ascii=False,
 193:         separators=(",", ":"),
 194:     ).encode("utf-8")
 195: 
 196:     # Build FileEntry list with content_type tags
 197:     file_entries: list[FileEntry] = []
 198:     content_type_by_path = {
 199:         FILE_SCOPE_DECISION: "scope_decision",
 200:         FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL: "evidence_pool",
 201:         FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT: "verified_report",
 202:         FILE_METADATA: "metadata",
 203:     }
 204:     for path, content in files_bytes.items():
 205:         ct = content_type_by_path.get(
 206:             path,
 207:             "source_snapshot" if path.startswith(SOURCES_DIR + "/") else "metadata",
 208:         )
 209:         file_entries.append(
 210:             FileEntry(
 211:                 path=path,
 212:                 sha256=_sha256_bytes(content),
 213:                 size_bytes=len(content),
 214:                 content_type=ct,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 215:             )
 216:         )
 217: 
 218:     # Sort entries deterministically for stable manifest output
 219:     file_entries.sort(key=lambda f: f.path)
 220: 
 221:     manifest = BundleManifest(
 222:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 223:         pool_id=report.pool_id,
 224:         report_id=report.report_id,
 225:         generator_model=report.generator_model,
 226:         polaris_version=POLARIS_VERSION,
 227:         files=file_entries,
 228:     )
 229:     return manifest, files_bytes
 230:

 232: def serialize_manifest_yaml(manifest: BundleManifest) -> bytes:
 233:     """Produce canonical YAML bytes for GPG signing.
 234: 
 235:     PyYAML default_flow_style=False + sort_keys=True keeps it stable
 236:     across re-serializations.
 237:     """
 238:     payload = manifest.model_dump(mode="json")
 239:     return yaml.safe_dump(
 240:         payload,
 241:         default_flow_style=False,
 242:         sort_keys=True,
 243:         allow_unicode=True,

 104:     """Map pipeline-A tier to SourceTier Literal. T4+/UNKNOWN → T3."""
 105:     upper = (raw or "").upper().strip()
 106:     if upper in ("T1", "T2", "T3"):
