 131:     invariant that verifier_pass=False forbids evaluator_agrees=True.
 132:     """
 133:     fields = sent.model_dump()
 134:     fields["verifier_pass"] = False
 135:     fields["drop_reason"] = "invalid_token"
 136:     fields["evaluator_agrees"] = False
 137:     return VerifiedSentence(**fields)
 138: 
 139: 
 140: def _evidence_ids_in_tokens(provenance_tokens: list[str]) -> set[str]:
 141:     out: set[str] = set()
 142:     for tok in provenance_tokens:
 143:         m = _PROV_TOKEN_RE.search(tok)
 144:         if m:
 145:             out.add(m.group(1))
 146:     return out
 147: 
 148: 
 149: def _tokens_to_strings(tokens: tuple[EvidenceSpanToken, ...]) -> list[str]:
 150:     return [f"[#ev:{t.evidence_id}:{t.start}-{t.end}]" for t in tokens]
 151: 
 152: 
 153: def _read_optional_json(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any] | list[Any] | None:
 154:     if not path.is_file():
 155:         return None
 156:     try:
 157:         return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 158:     except json.JSONDecodeError:
 159:         return None
 160: 
 161: 
 162: def _full_text_for_evidence_id(
 163:     evidence_id: str,
 164:     evidence_pool_raw: dict[str, Any] | list[Any] | None,
 165: ) -> str | None:
 166:     """Lookup evidence body in evidence_pool.json (Codex iter-2 P2 Q4).
 167: 
 168:     Pipeline-A's persisted field is commonly `direct_quote`, not full_text.
 169:     """
 170:     if evidence_pool_raw is None:
 171:         return None
 172:     sources = (
 173:         evidence_pool_raw.get("sources") if isinstance(evidence_pool_raw, dict)
 174:         else evidence_pool_raw
 175:     )
 176:     if not isinstance(sources, list):
 177:         return None
 178:     for src in sources:
 179:         if not isinstance(src, dict):
 180:             continue
 181:         if src.get("evidence_id") == evidence_id or src.get("source_id") == evidence_id:
 182:             return (
 183:                 src.get("full_text")
 184:                 or src.get("direct_quote")
 185:                 or src.get("snippet")
 186:             )
 187:     return None
 188: 
 189: 
 190: def _parse_iso(value: Any) -> datetime | None:
 191:     if not value:
 192:         return None
 193:     if isinstance(value, datetime):
 194:         return value
 195:     try:
 196:         return datetime.fromisoformat(str(value).replace("Z", "+00:00"))
 197:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
 198:         return None
 199: 
 200: 
 201: def build_slice_chain(
 202:     artifact_dir: Path,
 203: ) -> tuple[ScopeDecision, EvidencePool, SliceChainVerifiedReport]:
 204:     """Convert a pipeline-A canonical artifact dir to slice-chain Pydantic models.
 205: 
 206:     Raises:
 207:         FileNotFoundError: artifact_dir missing required canonical files
 208:         SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError: sovereignty cascade leaves no
 209:             non-dropped sections (cannot ship a bundle for this run)
 210:     """
 211:     air = load_audit_ir(artifact_dir)
 212:     manifest_raw = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 213:     evidence_pool_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "evidence_pool.json")
 214: 
 215:     # ─── 1. ScopeDecision ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
 216:     decision_id = (
 217:         (manifest_raw.get("scope") or {}).get("decision_id")
 218:         or manifest_raw.get("external_run_id")
 219:         or str(uuid.uuid4())
 220:     )
 221:     scope_class = _derive_scope_class(
 222:         manifest_raw.get("domain"),
 223:         (manifest_raw.get("scope") or {}).get("classification"),
 224:     )
 225:     decision = ScopeDecision(
 226:         decision_id=decision_id,
 227:         status="in_scope",
 228:         scope_class=scope_class,
 229:         ambiguity_axes=[],
 230:         clarifications_needed=[],
 231:         provenance={
 232:             "classifier_layer": "pipeline_a_v30",
 233:             "artifact_dir": str(artifact_dir),
 234:         },
 235:     )
 236: 
 237:     # ─── 2. EvidencePool (sovereignty-filtered) ───────────────────────────
 238:     sources: list[Source] = []
 239:     cleared_evidence_ids: set[str] = set()
 240:     for entry in air.bibliography:
 241:         # Tier-1 is legal-cleared by default; non-T1 requires explicit clearance
 242:         # in evidence_pool.json provenance.legal_cleared = True (Phase 2 hook).
 243:         canonical_tier, raw_tier = _normalize_tier(entry.tier)
 244:         is_legal_cleared = canonical_tier == SourceTier.T1
 245:         if not is_legal_cleared:
 246:             continue  # exclude — sovereignty_guard would reject otherwise
 247:         full_text = _full_text_for_evidence_id(entry.evidence_id, evidence_pool_raw)
 248:         sources.append(Source(
 249:             source_id=entry.evidence_id,
 250:             url=entry.url,
 251:             domain=_url_domain(entry.url),
 252:             tier=canonical_tier,
 253:             title=entry.statement[:200] or "Untitled",
 254:             snippet=entry.statement[:1000] or "n/a",
 255:             full_text_available=full_text is not None,
 256:             full_text=full_text,
 257:             provenance={
 258:                 "legal_cleared": True,
 259:                 "raw_tier": raw_tier,
 260:             },
 261:             retracted=False,
 262:         ))
 263:         cleared_evidence_ids.add(entry.evidence_id)
 264: 
 265:     retrieval_block = manifest_raw.get("retrieval", {}) or {}
 266:     started_utc = _parse_iso(retrieval_block.get("started_at")) or datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 267:     finished_utc = _parse_iso(retrieval_block.get("finished_at")) or started_utc
 268:     pool = EvidencePool(
 269:         pool_id=retrieval_block.get("pool_id") or str(uuid.uuid4()),
 270:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 271:         sources=sources,
 272:         adequacy=AdequacyVerdict(
 273:             is_adequate=True,
 274:             adequacy_score=1.0,
 275:             failure_reason=None,
 276:         ),
 277:         queries_executed=retrieval_block.get("queries_executed", []) or [],
 278:         retrieval_started_at_utc=started_utc,
 279:         retrieval_finished_at_utc=finished_utc,
 280:         latency_ms=int(retrieval_block.get("latency_ms") or 0),
 281:         cost_usd=float(air.manifest.cost_usd or 0.0),
 282:     )
 283: 
 284:     # ─── 3. VerifiedReport (sovereignty cascade) ──────────────────────────
 285:     sections: list[Section] = []
 286:     for air_section in air.verified_report.sections:
 287:         kept: list[VerifiedSentence] = []
 288:         for air_sent in air_section.sentences:
 289:             sc_sent = _air_sentence_to_slice_chain(air_sent)
 290:             cited_ids = _evidence_ids_in_tokens(sc_sent.provenance_tokens)
 291:             if not cited_ids or cited_ids.issubset(cleared_evidence_ids):
 292:                 kept.append(sc_sent)
 293:             else:
 294:                 kept.append(_redact_sentence(sc_sent))
 295:         pass_count = sum(1 for s in kept if s.verifier_pass)
 296:         section_status: SectionStatus = (
 297:             "dropped" if pass_count == 0 else "verified"
 298:         )
 299:         sections.append(Section(
 300:             section_id=_slugify(air_section.title) or f"section_{len(sections)}",
 301:             section_title=air_section.title or f"Section {len(sections)}",
 302:             verified_sentences=kept,
 303:             section_verify_pass_rate=pass_count / max(len(kept), 1),
 304:             section_status=section_status,
 305:         ))
 306: 
 307:     non_dropped = [s for s in sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]
 308:     if not non_dropped:
 309:         raise SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError(
 310:             "every section dropped after sovereignty cascade; bundle cannot be assembled"
 311:         )
 312: 
 313:     overall = sum(s.section_verify_pass_rate for s in non_dropped) / len(non_dropped)
 314:     # Codex diff iter-1 P2-001 fix: partial_* runs still have kept sections;
 315:     # they're "success-with-degradation" not "no_verified_sections" aborts.
 316:     # PipelineVerdict Literal accepts success | abort_no_verified_sections;
 317:     # collapse partial_* into "success" since the pipeline did produce kept
 318:     # content (the degradation is recorded on the manifest, not the verdict).
 319:     manifest_status = air.manifest.status or ""
 320:     if manifest_status == "success" or manifest_status.startswith("partial_"):
 321:         pipeline_verdict: PipelineVerdict = "success"
 322:     else:
 323:         pipeline_verdict = "abort_no_verified_sections"
 324:     models_block = manifest_raw.get("models") or {}
 325:     report = SliceChainVerifiedReport(
 326:         report_id=air.manifest.run_id,
 327:         pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 328:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 329:         sections=sections,
 330:         overall_verify_pass_rate=overall,
 331:         pipeline_verdict=pipeline_verdict,
 332:         generator_model=models_block.get("generator") or "unknown",
 333:         evaluator_model=models_block.get("evaluator") or "strict_verify_v1",
 334:         family_segregation_passed=True,
 335:         verifier_pass_threshold=0.4,
 336:         started_at_utc=started_utc,
 337:         finished_at_utc=finished_utc,
 338:         latency_ms=int(retrieval_block.get("latency_ms") or 0),
 339:         cost_usd=float(air.manifest.cost_usd or 0.0),
 340:     )
 341:     return decision, pool, report
 342: 
 343: 
 344: def _air_sentence_to_slice_chain(air_sent: AuditIRSentence) -> VerifiedSentence:
 345:     """AuditIR ReportSentence → slice-chain VerifiedSentence."""
 346:     failure = air_sent.failure_reasons[0] if air_sent.failure_reasons else None
 347:     return VerifiedSentence(
 348:         section_id=_slugify(air_sent.section) or "section",
 349:         sentence_text=air_sent.text or "n/a",
 350:         provenance_tokens=_tokens_to_strings(air_sent.tokens),
 351:         verifier_pass=bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 352:         drop_reason=_normalize_drop_reason(failure) if not air_sent.is_verified else None,
 353:         evaluator_agrees=bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 354:         is_synthesis_claim=len(air_sent.tokens) == 0 and bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 355:     )
 356: 
 357: 
 358: def _url_domain(url: str) -> str:
 359:     """Extract host for the Source.domain field. Falls back to 'unknown'."""
 360:     from urllib.parse import urlparse
 361:     try:
 362:         return urlparse(str(url)).netloc or "unknown"
 363:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — defensive: never raise during bridge
 364:         return "unknown"

 366: 
 367: def _slugify(text: str) -> str:
 368:     return re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", (text or "").lower()).strip("_")[:60]

   1: """Source snapshot — collects every cited source's text into the bundle.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md` §"snapshot_sources".
   4: 
   5: Walks every kept VerifiedSentence across every non-dropped Section in
   6: the VerifiedReport, extracts the unique source_ids referenced by their
   7: provenance tokens, then pulls the full_text (or snippet fallback) from
   8: the EvidencePool.
   9: 
  10: The snapshotted text is what makes the bundle independently verifiable
  11: offline: a third party can re-run strict_verify against the bundle's
  12: content without re-fetching from the original source URLs (which may
  13: have changed since retrieval).
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: from typing import NamedTuple
  19: 
  20: from polaris_graph.generator2.provenance import extract_tokens
  21: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import VerifiedReport
  22: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool, Source
  23: 
  24: 
  25: class SnapshotEntry(NamedTuple):
  26:     """Snapshot text plus the reachable character count (excludes appended truncation note)."""
  27: 
  28:     text: str
  29:     reachable_chars: int
  30: 
  31: 
  32: # Cap each source's text to keep the bundle bounded. 200KB per source
  33: # is enough for a typical full-text article; a Cochrane systematic
  34: # review with all appendices may need more — adjust if production
  35: # data shows truncation hits the audit_quality_gate.
  36: MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES = 200 * 1024  # 200 KB
  37: 
  38: SOURCE_TRUNCATION_NOTE_TEMPLATE = (
  39:     "\n\n[POLARIS audit-bundle truncation notice: source text truncated "
  40:     "from {original_size} to {truncated_size} bytes per "
  41:     "MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES policy.]"
  42: )
  43: 
  44: 
  45: def _cited_source_ids(report: VerifiedReport) -> set[str]:
  46:     """Collect source_ids from provenance tokens of every kept sentence
  47:     in every non-dropped section.
  48: 
  49:     Dropped sentences are excluded — we don't want to ship snapshots
  50:     for sources that didn't survive verification.
  51:     """
  52:     out: set[str] = set()
  53:     for section in report.sections:
  54:         if section.section_status == "dropped":
  55:             continue
  56:         for sentence in section.verified_sentences:
  57:             if not sentence.verifier_pass:
  58:                 continue
  59:             for token_str in sentence.provenance_tokens:
  60:                 tokens = extract_tokens(token_str)
  61:                 for tok in tokens:
  62:                     out.add(tok.source_id)
  63:     return out
  64: 
  65: 
  66: def _snapshot_text(source: Source) -> str:
  67:     """Return the text to snapshot for one source.
  68: 
  69:     Prefers full_text; falls back to snippet. Truncates at
  70:     MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES with an audit-visible note appended so
  71:     re-verifiers see why the span may not resolve.
  72:     """
  73:     text = source.full_text if source.full_text is not None else source.snippet
  74:     text_bytes = text.encode("utf-8")
  75:     if len(text_bytes) <= MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES:
  76:         return text
  77: 
  78:     # Truncate to MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES respecting UTF-8 boundaries.
  79:     truncated = text_bytes[:MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES]
  80:     # Walk back continuation bytes (10xxxxxx). The first non-continuation
  81:     # byte we hit is either a single-byte ASCII char (0xxxxxxx, complete)
  82:     # or a multi-byte start byte (11xxxxxx). If it's a start byte, the
  83:     # codepoint is incomplete because we already trimmed the continuations
  84:     # — drop the start byte too.
  85:     while truncated and (truncated[-1] & 0xC0) == 0x80:
  86:         truncated = truncated[:-1]
  87:     if truncated and (truncated[-1] & 0x80) and (truncated[-1] & 0x40):
  88:         truncated = truncated[:-1]
  89:     note = SOURCE_TRUNCATION_NOTE_TEMPLATE.format(
  90:         original_size=len(text_bytes),
  91:         truncated_size=len(truncated),
  92:     )
  93:     return truncated.decode("utf-8") + note
  94: 
  95: 
  96: def snapshot_sources(
  97:     report: VerifiedReport,
  98:     pool: EvidencePool,
  99: ) -> dict[str, str]:
 100:     """Return {source_id: snapshot_text} for every source cited in the
 101:     report's kept sentences.
 102: 
 103:     Source_ids that appear in tokens but are not present in the pool
 104:     are silently skipped (strict_verify already rejected those sentences,
 105:     so they shouldn't have made it through; defensive coding).
 106:     """
 107:     needed = _cited_source_ids(report)
 108:     pool_index: dict[str, Source] = {s.source_id: s for s in pool.sources}
 109: 
 110:     out: dict[str, str] = {}
 111:     for source_id in needed:
 112:         source = pool_index.get(source_id)
 113:         if source is None:
 114:             # Should not happen post-strict-verify; defensive skip
 115:             continue
 116:         out[source_id] = _snapshot_text(source)
 117:     return out
 118: 
 119: 
 120: def snapshot_size_bytes(snapshots: dict[str, str]) -> int:
 121:     """Total bytes across all snapshots — useful for bundle-size checks."""
 122:     return sum(len(text.encode("utf-8")) for text in snapshots.values())
 123: 
 124: 
 125: def _snapshot_entry(source: Source) -> SnapshotEntry:
 126:     """Snapshot one source returning text + reachable_chars (excl. truncation note)."""
 127:     text = source.full_text if source.full_text is not None else source.snippet
 128:     text_bytes = text.encode("utf-8")
 129:     if len(text_bytes) <= MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES:
 130:         return SnapshotEntry(text=text, reachable_chars=len(text))
 131:     truncated = text_bytes[:MAX_SOURCE_TEXT_BYTES]
 132:     while truncated and (truncated[-1] & 0xC0) == 0x80:
 133:         truncated = truncated[:-1]
 134:     if truncated and (truncated[-1] & 0x80) and (truncated[-1] & 0x40):
 135:         truncated = truncated[:-1]
 136:     body = truncated.decode("utf-8")
 137:     note = SOURCE_TRUNCATION_NOTE_TEMPLATE.format(
 138:         original_size=len(text_bytes), truncated_size=len(truncated)
 139:     )
 140:     return SnapshotEntry(text=body + note, reachable_chars=len(body))
 141: 
 142: 
 143: def snapshot_sources_with_reachable(
 144:     report: VerifiedReport, pool: EvidencePool
 145: ) -> dict[str, SnapshotEntry]:
 146:     """Like snapshot_sources but returns SnapshotEntry tuples (text + reachable_chars)."""
 147:     needed = _cited_source_ids(report)
 148:     pool_index: dict[str, Source] = {s.source_id: s for s in pool.sources}
 149:     out: dict[str, SnapshotEntry] = {}
 150:     for source_id in needed:
 151:         source = pool_index.get(source_id)
 152:         if source is None:
 153:             continue
 154:         out[source_id] = _snapshot_entry(source)
 155:     return out

   1: """EvidencePool schema for slice 002 (clinical retrieval).
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_002/architecture_proposal.md` §"Data contracts".
   4: Defines the canonical Pydantic types produced by the slice 002 clinical
   5: retriever and consumed by future slice 003 generation:
   6: 
   7:     ScopeDecision (slice 001)
   8:         ↓
   9:     process_retrieval()  (slice 002 — orchestrator, later PR)
  10:         ↓
  11:     EvidencePool (this module)
  12:         ↓
  13:     [slice 003 generator — future]
  14: 
  15: Pure-types module: no I/O, no network, no LLM calls. Validation only.
  16: 
  17: Slice 002 lives in `polaris_graph.retrieval2` (note the `2`) to keep
  18: clear separation from the heritage `polaris_graph.retrieval` substrate
  19: (live_retriever, source_registry, etc.) which serves the legacy honest-
  20: rebuild pipeline. The two coexist by design per PLAN.md §4.

  33: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  34: # Source tier enum
  35: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  36: 
  37: class SourceTier(str, Enum):
  38:     """Three-tier source classification per architecture proposal.
  39: 
  40:     T1 — regulatory + Cochrane systematic reviews. Highest evidentiary weight.
  41:     T2 — peer-reviewed primary research (RCTs, cohort studies, meta-analyses).
  42:     T3 — registries, clinical guidelines, government health agencies.
  43:     """
  44: 
  45:     T1 = "T1"
  46:     T2 = "T2"
  47:     T3 = "T3"
  48: 
  49: 
  50: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  51: # Source
  52: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  53: 
  54: class Source(BaseModel):
  55:     """A single retrieved clinical source.
  56: 
  57:     `full_text` is None at retrieval time and populated lazily by the
  58:     fetcher when downstream stages need the body. `snippet` is always
  59:     populated (first ~500 chars of relevant section) so quick adequacy
  60:     + tier classification can run without a second HTTP round-trip.
  61:     """
  62: 
  63:     source_id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
  64:     url: HttpUrl
  65:     domain: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=255)
  66:     tier: SourceTier
  67:     title: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=1000)
  68:     publication_date: date | None = None
  69:     authors: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list, max_length=200)
  70:     snippet: str = Field(min_length=0, max_length=2000)
  71:     full_text_available: bool = False
  72:     full_text: str | None = None
  73:     fetched_at_utc: datetime = Field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc))
  74:     provenance: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
  75:     retracted: bool = Field(
  76:         default=False,
  77:         description=(
  78:             "True iff source has been retracted post-publication "
  79:             "(I-f5-007). Default False — populated by future "
  80:             "CrossRef/Retraction Watch lookup. Today's retrieval "
  81:             "pipeline does not check; field is the surface for that "
  82:             "future wiring."
  83:         ),
  84:     )
  85: 
  86:     @field_validator("domain")
  87:     @classmethod
  88:     def _domain_lowercase(cls, v: str) -> str:
  89:         return v.strip().lower()
  90: 
  91:     @field_validator("authors")
  92:     @classmethod
  93:     def _authors_no_blanks(cls, v: list[str]) -> list[str]:
  94:         return [a.strip() for a in v if a and a.strip()]
  95: 
  96: 
  97: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  98: # Adequacy verdict
  99: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 100: 
 101: class AdequacyVerdict(BaseModel):
 102:     """Output of the corpus adequacy gate.
 103: 
 104:     `is_adequate=True` ⇒ pool may flow to slice 003 generation.
 105:     `is_adequate=False` + `failure_reason` populated ⇒ pipeline aborts
 106:     upstream of generation; UI surfaces the failure_reason verbatim.
 107:     """
 108: 
 109:     is_adequate: bool
 110:     sources_per_tier: dict[SourceTier, int] = Field(default_factory=dict)
 111:     min_required_per_tier: dict[SourceTier, int] = Field(default_factory=dict)
 112:     failure_reason: str | None = None
 113: 
 114:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 115:     def _check_failure_reason_consistency(self) -> "AdequacyVerdict":
 116:         if self.is_adequate is False and not self.failure_reason:
 117:             raise ValueError(
 118:                 "failure_reason is required when is_adequate=False"
 119:             )
 120:         if self.is_adequate is True and self.failure_reason:
 121:             raise ValueError(
 122:                 "failure_reason must be None when is_adequate=True"
 123:             )
 124:         return self
 125: 
 126: 
 127: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 128: # EvidencePool
 129: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 130: 
 131: class EvidencePool(BaseModel):
 132:     """The slice 002 output. Bound to a specific ScopeDecision via decision_id.
 133: 
 134:     `pool_id` is fresh per retrieval run; `decision_id` is the FK back to
 135:     the slice 001 ScopeDecision that triggered retrieval. Same decision +
 136:     same retrieval call may produce different pools across runs (sources
 137:     move, registries update); pool_id distinguishes them.
 138:     """
 139: 
 140:     pool_id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
 141:     decision_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
 142:     sources: list[Source] = Field(default_factory=list)
 143:     adequacy: AdequacyVerdict
 144:     queries_executed: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list, max_length=50)
 145:     retrieval_started_at_utc: datetime
 146:     retrieval_finished_at_utc: datetime
 147:     latency_ms: int = Field(ge=0)
 148:     cost_usd: float = Field(ge=0.0)
 149: 
 150:     @field_validator("retrieval_finished_at_utc")
 151:     @classmethod
 152:     def _finished_after_started(cls, v: datetime, info) -> datetime:
 153:         started = info.data.get("retrieval_started_at_utc")
 154:         if started is not None and v < started:
 155:             raise ValueError(
 156:                 "retrieval_finished_at_utc must be >= retrieval_started_at_utc"
 157:             )
 158:         return v
 159: 
 160:     def sources_by_tier(self, tier: SourceTier) -> list[Source]:
 161:         return [s for s in self.sources if s.tier == tier]
 162:

 170: 
 171:     Distinct from `EvidencePool { adequacy: { is_adequate: False } }`,
 172:     which signals retrieval ran but produced an inadequate corpus.
 173:     """

 175:     error: bool = True
 176:     code: str  # 'wrong_status' | 'wrong_scope_class' | 'fetch_backend_unavailable'
 177:     message: str
 178:     decision_id: str | None = None

 succeeded in 956ms:
   1: """VerifiedReport schema for slice 003 (generator + strict-verify).
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_003/architecture_proposal.md` §"verified_report.py".
   4: 
   5: Pure-types module. No I/O, no LLM, no network. Slice 003's
   6: process_generation() consumes an EvidencePool (slice 002 output) and
   7: produces a VerifiedReport, which slice 004 will export as an audit
   8: bundle.
   9: 
  10: Lives in `polaris_graph.generator2` (note the `2`) to keep separation
  11: from heritage `polaris_graph.generator` (multi_section, live_deepseek)
  12: which serves the legacy honest-rebuild pipeline. Coexistence by design
  13: per PLAN.md §4 Heritage Import.
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: import uuid
  19: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  20: from typing import Literal
  21: 
  22: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator, model_validator

  25: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  26: # Type literals
  27: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  28: 
  29: SectionStatus = Literal["verified", "regenerated", "dropped"]
  30: """Per-section outcome from strict_verify:
  31: 
  32: - "verified": original generation passed >=verifier_pass_threshold of
  33:   sentences strict-verified
  34: - "regenerated": original failed; regeneration attempt passed
  35: - "dropped": both attempts failed; section excluded from final report
  36: """
  37: 
  38: PipelineVerdict = Literal["success", "abort_no_verified_sections"]
  39: """Top-level verdict per CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 4."""
  40: 
  41: AssertionSurface = Literal[
  42:     "prose",
  43:     "table",
  44:     "summary_bullet",
  45:     "limitation",
  46:     "caption",
  47:     "heading",
  48: ]
  49: """Render-surface kind of a verified assertion (I-f5-009).
  50: 
  51: Per Carney plan §F: every assertion-bearing surface in a verified report
  52: must be gated-and-clickable through the Inspector OR explicitly marked
  53: ungated. Today's generator emits only "prose"; future Issues populate
  54: the other 5 surfaces as the generator learns to label table cells,
  55: summary bullets, etc."""
  56: 
  57: DropReason = Literal[
  58:     "invalid_token",       # token doesn't reference a known source_id
  59:     "span_out_of_range",   # span_start > span_end or > len(full_text)
  60:     "numeric_mismatch",    # decimal in sentence not present in cited span
  61:     "overlap_too_low",     # < min_content_overlap shared content words
  62:     "no_provenance_token", # sentence has no [#ev:...:start-end] tokens
  63:     "entailment_failed",   # I-bug-092: span does not entail sentence (semantic check)
  64: ]
  65: 
  66: 
  67: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  68: # VerifiedSentence — atomic verified unit
  69: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  70: 
  71: class VerifiedSentence(BaseModel):
  72:     """A single sentence emitted by the generator after strict-verify.
  73: 
  74:     Sentences that fail strict_verify are still represented here with
  75:     `verifier_pass=False` and a `drop_reason`, so the audit bundle can
  76:     surface "what got proposed and dropped" alongside "what shipped."
  77:     """
  78: 
  79:     section_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
  80:     sentence_text: str = Field(min_length=1)
  81:     provenance_tokens: list[str] = Field(
  82:         default_factory=list,
  83:         description="Token strings of form '[#ev:<source_id>:<start>-<end>]'",
  84:     )
  85:     verifier_pass: bool
  86:     drop_reason: DropReason | None = None
  87:     evaluator_agrees: bool | None = Field(
  88:         default=None,
  89:         description=(
  90:             "Two-family evaluator agreement per CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 1. "
  91:             "True = evaluator confirms generator claim; False = evaluator "
  92:             "disagrees; None = pending (no evaluator pass yet). At rule-based "
  93:             "stage this mirrors verifier_pass; future Issue plugs in the "
  94:             "real two-family LLM judge to populate this independently."
  95:         ),
  96:     )
  97:     assertion_surface: AssertionSurface = Field(
  98:         default="prose",
  99:         description=(
 100:             "Render-surface kind per I-f5-009. Default 'prose' preserves "
 101:             "back-compat with all existing fixtures. Non-prose values are "
 102:             "populated by future generator wiring (table cells, summary "
 103:             "bullets, limitations, captions, headings); the Inspector gates "
 104:             "all six surfaces equally."
 105:         ),
 106:     )
 107:     evaluator_disagreement: "EvaluatorDisagreement | None" = Field(
 108:         default=None,
 109:         description=(
 110:             "Optional detail when evaluator_agrees=False (I-f9-002). "
 111:             "Carries the evaluator's competing reading of the same evidence "
 112:             "so the EvaluatorPane can render generator-vs-evaluator side-by-side."
 113:         ),
 114:     )
 115:     contradiction: "ContradictionSignal | None" = Field(
 116:         default=None,
 117:         description=(
 118:             "Optional contradiction signal (I-f8-001). When present, "
 119:             "≥2 sources cited for this sentence disagree on the claim. "
 120:             "Default None preserves back-compat. Future Issue (F8-002+) "
 121:             "wires real detection into the generator."
 122:         ),
 123:     )
 124:     is_synthesis_claim: bool = Field(
 125:         default=False,
 126:         description=(
 127:             "True iff sentence is a synthesis claim (e.g., a discussion "
 128:             "paragraph summarizing across sources without quoting any one). "
 129:             "Synthesis claims have no provenance_tokens by definition; "
 130:             "non-synthesis kept sentences MUST have ≥1 provenance token. "
 131:             "Today's generator defaults to False; future Issue may wire the "
 132:             "prompt template to label synthesis sentences explicitly."
 133:         ),
 134:     )
 135: 
 136:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 137:     def _drop_reason_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedSentence":
 138:         if self.verifier_pass is False and self.drop_reason is None:
 139:             raise ValueError(
 140:                 "drop_reason is required when verifier_pass=False"
 141:             )
 142:         if self.verifier_pass is True and self.drop_reason is not None:
 143:             raise ValueError(
 144:                 "drop_reason must be None when verifier_pass=True"
 145:             )
 146:         return self
 147: 
 148:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 149:     def _evaluator_agreement_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedSentence":
 150:         if self.verifier_pass is False and self.evaluator_agrees is True:
 151:             raise ValueError(
 152:                 "evaluator_agrees=True is forbidden when verifier_pass=False "
 153:                 "(rule-based dropped the sentence; evaluator cannot pass it "
 154:                 "without contradicting strict-verify)"
 155:             )
 156:         return self
 157: 
 158:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 159:     def _synthesis_claim_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedSentence":
 160:         if self.is_synthesis_claim and self.verifier_pass is False:
 161:             raise ValueError(
 162:                 "is_synthesis_claim=True requires verifier_pass=True "
 163:                 "(synthesis claims either ship or are dropped before reaching "
 164:                 "this record)"
 165:             )
 166:         if self.is_synthesis_claim and len(self.provenance_tokens) > 0:
 167:             raise ValueError(
 168:                 "is_synthesis_claim=True requires provenance_tokens=[] "
 169:                 "(synthesis claims have no specific provenance — that's the "
 170:                 "definition)"
 171:             )
 172:         if (
 173:             not self.is_synthesis_claim
 174:             and self.verifier_pass is True
 175:             and len(self.provenance_tokens) == 0
 176:         ):
 177:             raise ValueError(
 178:                 "kept non-synthesis sentence requires ≥1 provenance token; "
 179:                 "set is_synthesis_claim=True for prose without specific "
 180:                 "provenance"
 181:             )
 182:         return self

 231: class ContradictionSide(BaseModel):

 233: 
 234:     Each side is a distinct cited source's position on the claim. Tier
 235:     + sample size + hedge language + PT08 flag inform reviewer judgment
 236:     of which side has the stronger evidentiary backing. evidence_type
 237:     (I-f8-005) tags the kind of source (trial, guideline, ...)."""
 238: 
 239:     source_id: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
 240:     source_tier: Literal["T1", "T2", "T3"]
 241:     sample_size: int | None = Field(default=None, ge=0)
 242:     hedge_language: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
 243:     pt08_flag: str | None = Field(default=None, max_length=50)
 244:     claim_excerpt: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=500)
 245:     evidence_type: ContradictionEvidenceType = Field(default="unspecified")
 246:     jurisdiction: Jurisdiction = Field(default="unspecified")

 249: ContradictionCategory = Literal[
 250:     "numeric",
 251:     "categorical",
 252:     "regulatory",
 253:     "temporal",
 254:     "jurisdictional",
 255:     "other",
 256: ]
 257: """I-f8-004 contradiction-category enum.
 258: 
 259: Distinguishes the kind of disagreement: numeric (dose/CI), categorical
 260: (approved/not approved), regulatory (FDA vs EMA), temporal (pre-2020 vs
 261: post-2020 evidence shift), jurisdictional (Canada vs US), other."""
 262: 
 263: 
 264: ContradictionKind = Literal["multi_source", "self_contradiction"]
 265: """I-f8-003 contradiction-kind discriminator.
 266: 
 267: `multi_source`: ≥2 distinct sources disagree (I-f8-001/002 case).
 268: `self_contradiction`: 1 source contradicts itself across spans/paragraphs."""
 269: 
 270: 
 271: class ContradictionSignal(BaseModel):
 272:     """Inline contradiction annotation per sentence (I-f8-001).
 273: 
 274:     Indicates ≥2 cited sources disagree on the claim in the sentence.
 275:     `sides` (added I-f8-002) carries the per-source detail consumed by
 276:     the ContradictionPane; empty preserves I-f8-001 back-compat.
 277:     `kind` (added I-f8-003) discriminates multi-source vs self-contradiction."""
 278: 
 279:     disagreeing_source_count: int = Field(ge=1, le=20)
 280:     summary: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=500)
 281:     sides: list[ContradictionSide] = Field(default_factory=list)
 282:     kind: ContradictionKind = Field(default="multi_source")
 283:     category: ContradictionCategory = Field(default="other")
 284: 
 285:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 286:     def _kind_count_consistency(self) -> "ContradictionSignal":
 287:         if self.kind == "multi_source":
 288:             if self.disagreeing_source_count < 2:
 289:                 raise ValueError(
 290:                     "kind='multi_source' requires "
 291:                     "disagreeing_source_count >= 2"
 292:                 )
 293:             if (
 294:                 self.sides
 295:                 and len(self.sides) != self.disagreeing_source_count
 296:             ):
 297:                 raise ValueError(
 298:                     "len(sides) must equal disagreeing_source_count for "
 299:                     "multi_source when sides is non-empty"
 300:                 )
 301:         else:  # self_contradiction
 302:             if self.disagreeing_source_count != 1:
 303:                 raise ValueError(
 304:                     "kind='self_contradiction' requires "
 305:                     "disagreeing_source_count == 1"
 306:                 )
 307:             if len(self.sides) < 2:
 308:                 raise ValueError(
 309:                     "kind='self_contradiction' requires sides with ≥2 "
 310:                     "entries representing distinct contradicting spans "
 311:                     "from the same source"
 312:                 )
 313:             distinct_source_ids = {s.source_id for s in self.sides}
 314:             if len(distinct_source_ids) != 1:
 315:                 raise ValueError(
 316:                     "kind='self_contradiction' requires all sides to "
 317:                     "reference the same source_id"
 318:                 )
 319:         return self
 320: 
 321: 
 322: GapReason = Literal[
 323:     "paywalled",
 324:     "no_oa",
 325:     "source_tier_ineligible",
 326:     "language_unavailable",
 327:     "retracted_only",
 328:     "jurisdiction_outside",
 329:     "not_indexed",
 330:     "embargoed",
 331:     "other",
 332: ]
 333: """Frozen taxonomy of frame-gap reasons (I-f7-002).
 334: 
 335: Replaces the free-text reason from I-f7-001. Forces consistent UI
 336: labels and analytics aggregation. `other` is the escape hatch — paired
 337: with `reason_detail` when it's used."""
 338: 
 339: 
 340: class FrameGap(BaseModel):
 341:     """A single uncovered entity in a frame coverage report."""
 342: 
 343:     entity_name: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
 344:     reason: GapReason
 345:     reason_detail: str | None = Field(
 346:         default=None,
 347:         max_length=500,
 348:         description=(
 349:             "Optional free-text supplement to the enum reason "
 350:             "(I-f7-002). Renders as 'Label: detail' in the panel."
 351:         ),
 352:     )
 353: 
 354: 
 355: class FrameCoverage(BaseModel):
 356:     """Top-of-report frame coverage summary (I-f7-001).
 357: 
 358:     Surfaces "X of N entities covered" with explicit gap reasons. Consumed
 359:     by the FrameCoveragePanel above the verified report. Optional on
 360:     VerifiedReport; older payloads without coverage render no panel."""
 361: 
 362:     covered_entity_count: int = Field(ge=0)
 363:     total_entity_count: int = Field(ge=0)
 364:     gaps: list[FrameGap] = Field(default_factory=list)
 365: 
 366:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 367:     def _counts_consistency(self) -> "FrameCoverage":
 368:         if self.covered_entity_count > self.total_entity_count:
 369:             raise ValueError(
 370:                 "covered_entity_count cannot exceed total_entity_count"
 371:             )
 372:         if (
 373:             self.covered_entity_count + len(self.gaps)
 374:             != self.total_entity_count
 375:         ):
 376:             raise ValueError(
 377:                 "covered_entity_count + len(gaps) must equal total_entity_count"
 378:             )
 379:         return self
 380:

 382: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 383: # Section
 384: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 385: 
 386: class Section(BaseModel):
 387:     """A report section (e.g. 'Population', 'Outcomes').
 388: 
 389:     `verified_sentences` includes both passed AND dropped sentences for
 390:     audit completeness; UI filters by `verifier_pass` when rendering the
 391:     user-facing report. `section_verify_pass_rate` is over all attempted
 392:     sentences (not just kept ones).
 393:     """
 394: 
 395:     section_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
 396:     section_title: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
 397:     verified_sentences: list[VerifiedSentence] = Field(default_factory=list)
 398:     section_verify_pass_rate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
 399:     section_status: SectionStatus
 400: 
 401:     def kept_sentences(self) -> list[VerifiedSentence]:
 402:         """Filter to sentences that passed strict_verify."""
 403:         return [s for s in self.verified_sentences if s.verifier_pass]

 406: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 407: # VerifiedReport
 408: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 409: 
 410: class VerifiedReport(BaseModel):
 411:     """The slice 003 output. Bound to a slice-002 pool via pool_id +
 412:     a slice-001 decision via decision_id. Same pool can produce different
 413:     reports across runs (LLM nondeterminism); report_id distinguishes them.
 414:     """
 415: 
 416:     report_id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
 417:     pool_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
 418:     decision_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
 419:     sections: list[Section] = Field(default_factory=list)
 420:     overall_verify_pass_rate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
 421:     pipeline_verdict: PipelineVerdict
 422:     generator_model: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
 423:     evaluator_model: str = Field(
 424:         min_length=1,
 425:         max_length=200,
 426:         description=(
 427:             "Two-family evaluator identifier per CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 1. "
 428:             "Rule-based stage value: 'strict_verify_v1'. When a real LLM "
 429:             "judge wires in (separate Issue), this becomes the OpenRouter "
 430:             "model id from a different training family than generator_model."
 431:         ),
 432:     )
 433:     family_segregation_passed: bool = Field(
 434:         default=True,
 435:         description=(
 436:             "True iff generator and evaluator are confirmed to be from "
 437:             "different training lineages (rule-based always True; future "
 438:             "two-family LLM judge invokes "
 439:             "openrouter_client.check_family_segregation)."
 440:         ),
 441:     )
 442:     verifier_pass_threshold: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
 443:     started_at_utc: datetime
 444:     finished_at_utc: datetime
 445:     latency_ms: int = Field(ge=0)
 446:     cost_usd: float = Field(ge=0.0)
 447:     frame_coverage: FrameCoverage | None = Field(
 448:         default=None,
 449:         description=(
 450:             "Optional top-of-report frame coverage summary (I-f7-001). "
 451:             "When present, the Inspector renders a panel above-the-fold "
 452:             "showing 'X of N entities covered' + each gap with reason. "
 453:             "Default None preserves back-compat with older payloads."
 454:         ),
 455:     )
 456: 
 457:     @field_validator("finished_at_utc")
 458:     @classmethod
 459:     def _finished_after_started(cls, v: datetime, info) -> datetime:
 460:         started = info.data.get("started_at_utc")
 461:         if started is not None and v < started:
 462:             raise ValueError(
 463:                 "finished_at_utc must be >= started_at_utc"
 464:             )
 465:         return v
 466: 
 467:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 468:     def _verdict_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedReport":
 469:         """If verdict=success, at least one section must be verified or
 470:         regenerated. If verdict=abort_no_verified_sections, every section
 471:         (if any) must be 'dropped' or sections may be empty."""
 472:         if self.pipeline_verdict == "success":
 473:             kept = [
 474:                 s for s in self.sections if s.section_status != "dropped"
 475:             ]
 476:             if not kept:
 477:                 raise ValueError(
 478:                     "pipeline_verdict='success' requires at least one "
 479:                     "non-dropped section"
 480:                 )
 481:         else:  # abort_no_verified_sections
 482:             for section in self.sections:
 483:                 if section.section_status != "dropped":
 484:                     raise ValueError(
 485:                         "pipeline_verdict='abort_no_verified_sections' "
 486:                         "requires all sections (if any) to be dropped"
 487:                     )
 488:         return self
 489: 
 490:     def kept_sections(self) -> list[Section]:
 491:         """Filter to non-dropped sections."""
 492:         return [s for s in self.sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]
 493:

 506:     decision_id: str | None = None
